It is hoped that a solution will be reached and an approval date will be set within a few days, so that all diplomatic relations such as the establishment of consulates and trade in Vietnam can be implemented according to law. (Special dispatch, 12th)

Tibetan Postal System 16

(Nanjing) The Tibetan postal service was established in the first year of the Republic of China and initially hired a British person to manage it. Up to now, the total postal route is about 10,000 kilometers. Due to the lack of railways and highways, postal delivery and transportation still use the courier station method. Mail carriers ride horses, which is about twice as fast as walking. There is a relay station every ninety miles, and each person travels four stations a day. A journey of a thousand miles takes a week to arrive, but it takes more than ten days in case of wind and snow. Official documents of the Tibetan government are delivered by special messengers and are not sent by mail. The Tibetan postal system has four types of services: ordinary, registered, parcel post, and money order. The minimum postage for correspondence is 7.5 fen, and the registration fee is 1.5 times that amount. For parcel post and money order, 25/1000 of the original value is charged. That is, for a value of 20 Tibetan coins, a postal fee of 5 Tibetan coins is required, and the same applies to money orders. The minimum postage stamp is 7.5 fen, divided into green, blue, and light red colors. The central image is of a lion stepping into a snowy mountain, with a sun and moon drawn on the upper left and right sides. Most are marked with both Tibetan and English characters. The business is not very developed at present, and the Tibetan government has an annual subsidy. (Special dispatch, 12th)

Han Fuju Telegraphed to Recommend Lin Jiqing as a Provincial Committee Member 17

(Jinan) Han Fuju telegraphed to recommend Lin Jiqing to succeed as a member of the Provincial Government Committee. Lin is from Laiyang and is a mining engineer from Lehigh University in the United States. He has served as the president of Qingdao University and the dean of the College of Arts and Sciences of Qilu University, and also as acting president. (Special dispatch, 12th)

(Qingdao) Fang Juehui arrived in Qingdao with Ge Guangting on the morning of the 12th. According to him, I have no mission here, and was just invited by Ge to visit here. I will go to Jinan on the evening of the 13th and then to Beiping to meet with He. (Telegram, 12th)

The Problem of China's Cultural Construction 18

The Necessity of Establishing More Research Institutes Quickly

Recently, a new awakening has emerged in domestic academic and public opinion circles regarding China's cultural construction. This is the necessity for China's academic culture to be independent. For example, Mr. Cai Yuanpei, Mr. Wang Yunwu, and Mr. Ren Hongjun have respectively advocated in the *Eastern Miscellany* and the *Education Magazine* that universities should establish research institutes so that university graduates who wish to pursue further studies do not have to go abroad for study. Furthermore, scholars in Shanghai, such as Mr. Wang Xinming and Mr. He Bingsong, have published articles and expressed their opinions in the *Cultural Construction Monthly* and the education news column of this newspaper, advocating "adopting the strengths of others and discarding their weaknesses" to put China in a leading position and seek cultural creation. This kind of awakening was not commonly seen before and is indeed a sign of progress in China's intellectual circles.

Since the opening of China to foreign trade, China has suffered from the invasion of foreign powers, not only losing faith in its inherent culture but also developing great doubts about the excellence of its national character. Consequently, without realizing it, people have paid sincere admiration and worship to everything foreign, while losing the confidence they should have in their own intelligence and strength. If one's spirit becomes a slave to others, then the desire to have creative abilities is like heading north to reach the south. In reality, the development of Chinese culture is less than two hundred years behind Western culture. That is, Western culture has already entered the era of mechanical industry, while we, due to our past isolation in the Far East, are still stagnating in the era of handicrafts and agriculture. As for spiritual culture, the difference is actually very small. This is a commonly recognized difference by sociologists and cultural historians. Therefore, China's backwardness today is by no means the result of the inferiority of its national character, but a temporary difference in historical development. If we can maintain faith and "catch up head-on," there is nothing we cannot achieve. Take Japan, our neighbor to the east. What culture did it have sixty or seventy years ago? But how long has it been now? It is already competing with Britain and the United States. It can be seen that if one believes in oneself and does not belittle oneself, one will surely be able to strive for progress. Therefore, in the future, if we want to seek the independence and construction of Chinese academic culture, we must take self-confidence as the key. Observing the recent speeches and proposals of the academic community, it is felt that they have a clear understanding of this point, which is really something to be congratulated on.

The progress of all countries in the world in terms of knowledge, thought, and technology is advancing day by day. For our country, which has always been backward, competing with them is like trying to catch up with the dust, and the sigh of being unable to reach is heard. Therefore, it is indeed difficult to seek independence in academic culture. However, if we can do our best to promote it, it is not without a solution. The most obvious is the absorption of foreign culture: (1) We should consider whether it is suitable for the current needs of the country. (2) We should follow the path of sacrificing the least and achieving the greatest effect to advance. Throughout history, our country has always regarded sending students abroad as the only way to absorb foreign culture. After completing their studies and returning to the country, they receive high attention from society, and their position is often uniquely superior. Therefore, for decades, they have been regarded as a special class in all aspects. As a result, young students all regard being able to study abroad as an honor, and they do not have time to ask whether their personal studies are suitable for the current needs of the country. As a result, what the country urgently needs are industrial and technical talents, while society is filled with talents in literature, philosophy, law, and politics. On the one hand, there is still a feeling of lack, and on the other hand, there is already a feeling of excess. It can be said that both the country and the individual suffer losses. Furthermore, although there is no shortage of students who truly want to go abroad to study in order to introduce world culture, those whose purpose is only to obtain a title actually account for a large proportion. Even from an economic point of view, it is not worth the loss. For subjects such as literature, philosophy, politics, and law, what is needed are books. With books, one can learn anywhere, without spending ten times the money spent domestically to go abroad for study. According to the latest announcement from the Ministry of Education, the number of Chinese students studying abroad in the past few years is about 3,700 or more, and those studying liberal arts account for more than 2,100. If we assume that the cost of each student studying abroad is 10,000 yuan, then the outflow of money amounts to as much as 37 million yuan. Moreover, the cost of liberal arts students is even greater than that of science students. With our country's annual trade deficit in international trade, the continuous outflow of cash, and the extremely difficult national economy, how can we bear this unplanned and uncontrolled waste? Therefore, we here hope that domestic universities will quickly establish research institutes, or expand the existing Academia Sinica, so that university graduates in the country who wish to pursue further studies will have somewhere to turn. At the same time, we must ensure that scholars who study social sciences do not have to study abroad, and that those who study science and engineering can also reduce the number of students studying abroad to the minimum. We must ensure that only those who are truly indispensable to going abroad are selected as scholars with profound knowledge to go abroad to study, or to conduct a short-term inspection. In this way, millions of dollars can be used for the equipment costs of various research institutes and academies of sciences every year.

With various research institutions in place, scholars can rely on them for research, experimentation, and invention. As a result, discoveries in academics and inventions in things and machinery will surely follow. Compared with the policy of studying abroad to carry knowledge, the gains and losses cannot be calculated by reason. We dare to believe that if this plan is used and accumulated over the years, it will surely enable China's academic culture to gradually advance to the realm of independence and creation.

Recent Situation of Chen Duxiu in Prison 32

He gets up at 6:00 AM, opens the door at 7:00, and walks in the small courtyard for half an hour, regardless of wind or rain, taking a few minutes of deep breaths. He eats breakfast at 8:00 AM and dinner at 4:00 PM. He eats twice a day, with rice and vegetables, as well as eggs and canned food, which he prepares himself, and occasionally eats a small amount of cod liver oil nourishing products. He goes to bed at 9:00 PM and reads books during the day, but is prohibited from reading newspapers. Prison officials do not absolutely prohibit Chen from meeting guests. Britain Plans to Propose Abolishing Military Clauses of the Treaty of Versailles 54

Disarmament Convention and Guarantee of Austrian Independence

Germany's Participation as a Major Condition

Simon Rushes Back from Geneva to Attend Cabinet Meeting

(London) Foreign Secretary Simon will rush back from Geneva on Monday to attend a Cabinet meeting, reportedly the most important since the end of the European War. The Cabinet will discuss a plan under which, after Germany agrees to accept the Disarmament Convention and participate in the Danube Agreement guaranteeing Austrian independence, the Allied powers victorious in the Great War would agree to abolish the military clauses of the Treaty of Versailles. Regarding this matter, there is much speculation in diplomatic circles about the attitude of the United States, because the treaty between the US and Germany stipulates that the US enjoys the rights of the military clauses in the Treaty of Versailles. If the Disarmament Convention can be established first, replacing the military clauses in the Treaty of Versailles, it is believed that the US will also, either alone or by joining the Disarmament Convention, recognize Germany's release from the military constraints of the treaty. (National Telegram, 12th)

(London) Foreign Secretary Simon is scheduled to leave Geneva tonight and return to the country, arriving tomorrow night. Once the Foreign Secretary arrives, the Cabinet will convene immediately to discuss (1) the Saar issue, (2) arms limitation, and (3) French Prime Minister Flandin and Laval's visit to Britain. Foreign Secretary Simon will likely travel to Geneva again within the next week. (Havas Telegram, 12th)

(London) The Times published an article proposing that "the military clauses of the Treaty of Versailles, or a unilateral declaration by Germany, should lose their effect under certain conditions. Such unilateral action should be prevented by the countries benefiting from the Treaty of Versailles." It is reported that British diplomatic authorities are currently studying a plan regarding this issue. What The Times said is only one aspect of it. The British plan believes that if the defeated countries in the European War want the victorious countries to abandon the rights contained in the treaty clauses, they must submit a formal request to the League of Nations. A formal request can only be accepted if made by a member state of the League of Nations. Supporters of this plan believe that only in this way can other countries' promises regarding Germany's equal rights to armaments and Germany's return to Geneva be simultaneously realized. That is, negotiations on an international convention limiting armaments can only proceed smoothly in this way. (Havas Telegram, 12th)

Building Peace Domestically

Equal International Cooperation

Expression by the Ambassador to London

(London) The German Ambassador to London, Hoesch, tonight, at a consulate banquet in Birmingham, expressed the attitude of Germany towards international conventions with extremely sincere words. He said that the new Germany now has two major goals: one is to build peace at home and enjoy honor abroad, and the other is that Germany is willing to engage in international affairs based on the principle of equal rights for all countries. There is no doubt about Germany's inclination towards peace. Germany sincerely hopes that Britain can gain a better understanding of Germany's new developments. The Great War was indeed tragic, but the indelible and countless bonds still exist and are reuniting us, which has proven to be more appropriate than commemorating the tragic war. (Reuters Telegram, 11th)

Preamble to the Rome Agreement Announced 57

Declaration of General Franco-Italian Policy

Mutual Consultation to Jointly Maintain Peace

(Paris) The Franco-Italian Convention signed in Rome on the 7th of this month contains four documents. The first document, the Preamble to the Franco-Italian Convention, is a declaration of general policy by the two governments. The full text of this declaration has been formally released by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and is recorded below. The other three documents have not yet been released.

"The French and Italian governments believe that the agreement concluded between the two countries today guarantees that certain unresolved issues between the two countries arising from previous agreements, especially those concerning the implementation of Article 13 of the London Agreement of April 26, 1915, can be resolved in principle. The French and Italian governments also believe that any future disputes that may arise between the two governments can be resolved through diplomatic channels, the Covenant of the League of Nations, the Statute of the Permanent Court of International Justice, and the procedures stipulated in general arbitration treaties. To this end, the governments jointly declare that they have decided to develop the traditional friendship that unites the two countries and to cooperate in a spirit of mutual trust to maintain universal peace. For the sake of this cooperation, the two governments should consult each other whenever necessary. Signed by Laval and Mussolini." (Havas Telegram, 11th)

League of Nations Urges Calm Among Residents on the Eve of the Saarland Vote 58

Term of the Three-Person Committee Extended

Handling Post-Vote Implementation Procedures

(Geneva) The League of Nations' message to the people of the Saar, passed unanimously by the Administrative Council this morning, has been issued. This is the first time since the establishment of the Administrative Council that it has issued a statement to the people of a particular region in the form of a declaration. The declaration states: "As Saar citizens prepare to vote, the League of Nations Administrative Council solemnly urges residents to adopt a calm and dignified attitude to demonstrate their awareness of the importance of this event, and to maintain the same attitude after the vote, and to await the Administrative Council's adoption of appropriate decisions in the shortest possible time." This morning, the Saar Regional Administrative Commission also reported to the League of Nations that the people's emotions were extremely excited, requesting action to inform the Saar people that the Administrative Council would continue to preside over everything and would not be negligent from the time the referendum results were announced until the consequences occurred. Now that the Administrative Council has extended the term of the three-person committee and directly issued a declaration to the Saar residents, its effect should be to stabilize people's minds. (Havas Telegram, 12th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council held a closed-door meeting this morning to discuss the Saarland issue. It was decided to extend the powers of the Saarland Three-Person Committee (appointed by the Administrative Council last year, composed of Italian representative Aloisi, Argentine representative Cantilo, and Spanish representative Madariaga). The purpose of this decision by the Administrative Council is to inform the Saar residents that all procedures regarding the interpretation and implementation of the referendum results will be handled by a supervisory body of a transcendent nature (i.e., the Three-Person Committee) specially entrusted by the Administrative Council. Saarbrücken, Saarland It is believed here that after the Referendum Committee reports the referendum results to the League of Nations Administrative Council, the Administrative Council will take various decisions, and its session will inevitably be extended for some time. The issues that the Administrative Council should resolve are as follows:

(1) The issue of the Saar region's sovereignty before the implementation of the referendum results. (2) Determine the date of the transfer of sovereignty with reference to the Saar Three-Person Committee's report of December 5 last year. According to the report, if the referendum results decide to return to Germany, the transition period should be at least one month. (3) The date of withdrawal of international troops. (4) The nationality and rights of Saar residents, and the right to choose nationality. (5) Other related issues, such as (A) the status of Saar regional civil servants. Regarding this, the Administrative Council passed a resolution on May 17, 1933, recognizing the original rights of civil servants, which should be guaranteed regardless of the referendum results. (B) Social insurance and property transfer methods when residents leave the area. (Havas Telegram, 12th)

German Front Has a Better Chance of Winning

The Force of the Maintaining Status Quo Faction Is Also Not Weak

Saarbrücken, Saarland Tonight, the anti-National Socialist newspapers are all headlined with optimistic words, including "Tomorrow we will defeat Hitler," and "Liberate ourselves from Germany's grasp," "Use maintaining the current situation to defeat Hitler." Now, those who enthusiastically support Hitler also admit that if there are too many votes supporting maintaining the current situation, it will greatly damage the German leader's prestige. Supporters of returning the Saarland to Germany hope that their votes will account for 80 percent of the total votes, but the opposition laughs at this, saying that this number is too high. As for the united front of the Socialist Party and the Communist Party, it is feared that it will be difficult to obtain 100,000 votes out of 540,000 votes. A certain Catholic newspaper that opposes Hitler today announced to its readers that the Pope has ordered the Saar Catholics to follow their conscience, but it is feared that many Catholics will regard patriotism as more important than everything else. At present, everyone is convinced that the referendum will not be hindered by riots, but the military and police are very closely guarded, without the slightest relaxation. Today, there is a heavy snowstorm here, and most enthusiasts are staying at home, so there is no crowd to welcome voters when they arrive at the polling stations. The surrounding areas of each polling station are heavily guarded by police, cavalry, and infantry. Today, only those who cannot go to the polling stations tomorrow due to official duties are allowed to vote. (Reuters Telegram, 12th)

Saarland's Return to Germany Will Affect Heavy Industry 67

Saarbrücken The "Grenzland" weekly published some secret reports by experts to the board of directors of various factories in the city of Neunkirchen, which are generally considered to be surprising. According to the report's observation, once the Saarland region decides to return to Germany, the factories will be affected in various ways. If the Saarland returns to Germany, the French border will be closed, preventing German metallurgical products from being easily imported. If this happens, German industry will lose its sales to France. The conclusion also states that the Neunkirchen steel mill, in which the two major German industrialists Ulf and Gurlmen have invested heavily, will increase its annual burden by 5,715,000 marks once the Saarland is under German rule. Its operating income will only be enough to cover some depreciation expenses. The reason is that the Saarland industry is tied to the French tariff system, and without iron sand from Lorraine, France, the Saarland steel mills will not be able to continue working. The only way to save it is to continue to maintain French sales. The report says that there is a possibility of engaging in beneficial negotiations on this matter, as France sells goods worth 120 million francs to the Saarland, while purchasing goods worth only 80 million francs from the Saarland. The report concludes: "The Saarland heavy industry should not allow the German Front to carry out propaganda at will in its factories, oppress workers, and organize nationalist demonstrations in the Chamber of Commerce. Once the Saarland returns to Germany, they will have to advise the board of directors of the following facts: (1) The return of the Saarland to Germany is tantamount to the destruction of heavy industry. (2) The return of the Saarland to Germany is tantamount to increasing unemployment and reducing wages. (3) The return of the Saarland to Germany is tantamount to economic suicide." (Havas Telegram, 11th)

Fourteen People Arrested in Chiba

Accused of Being Suspected Spies

(Tokyo) Yesterday, the Chiba Prefectural Police Department secretly ordered police stations within the prefecture to arrest overseas Chinese and send them to the police department before 8:00 AM on the 13th. Today, fourteen overseas Chinese were unreasonably arrested and successively escorted to Chiba, the prefectural capital. It is said that the reason for the Japanese police's arrest of the overseas Chinese is the false accusation that they are suspected spies. After the arrest, they will be forced to return to their home country in the form of voluntary repatriation, without taking the form of deportation because there is no legal basis for deportation. Among the arrested overseas Chinese, the most resided in the military stronghold of Tateyama. It is said that because the Japanese police have no legitimate reason to deport overseas Chinese, they plan to successively accuse them of being spies and sweep away overseas Chinese from military strongholds throughout the country. (Hualian Telegram, 12th)

British Sheffield Factory Rushes to Manufacture Armaments Day and Night 76

Japanese Iron and Steel Industry is Particularly Developed

(London) According to the Hochi Shimbun, the Sheffield steel factory manufactured 100,000 tons (about one-tenth of the factory's total output) of steel for armaments in 1934. According to members of the local Chamber of Commerce, the factory has been busy manufacturing armaments since before the Great War, and recently received orders from both the Army and Air Force, rushing to produce special light steel and other bulletproof alloys. The factory has become the center of armament production. Currently, ten commissioners from both the Army and Air Force are stationed at the factory to supervise production. (Guomin Telegram, 12th)

(Tokyo) Japan's iron and steel industry remains strong. The estimated demand for pig iron this year is 1.6 million tons. Japan proper and "Manchukuo" can supply 1 million tons, and the rest must be supplied by foreign countries. The Pig Iron National Policy Committee met on the 11th and decided to petition the government to temporarily exempt foreign pig iron from import tariffs to alleviate the shortage of pig iron. Minister of Commerce Machida also understood this matter and has stated that the authorities will work hard to properly handle the pig iron issue. (Rengo Telegram, 12th)

Astronomical Phenomena Predict Warplanes are Imminent 77

Sunspots Emit Electromagnetic Force

Capable of Making Human Minds Anxious and Irritable

(Paris) Maurice, the director of the Baojian Observatory, observed the sun and moon today with a huge telescope and predicted the crisis of a latent world war in 1936 and 1937. Maurice claimed that he does not believe in astrology, and his prediction is based on astronomy. Maurice said that sunspots constantly emit electric and magnetic forces. This electromagnetic force can make people restless and irritable, so that the smallest international disputes can lead to war. Maurice also cited the history of the 1900 war to prove his theory. When the sun is still, the world can celebrate peace and prosperity, and people devote themselves to art and culture. The early periods of 1900, 1910, and 1920 were periods when the sun was still. However, after sunspots appeared, wars broke out in the world. Sunspots appear on the sun once every eleven years. The Moroccan War in 1905 and the World War in 1914 also coincided with this solar activity. Maurice also stated that sunspots can also cause other disasters. In 1936 and 1937, the world will also experience gales, earthquakes, gout, and heart diseases. Maurice concluded that only the sun and moon in the universe can affect the earth, the sun because of its large size, and the moon because of its closest distance to the earth. (Guomin Telegram, 11th)

US Supreme Court Debates the Abolition of Gold Clauses 78

The Situation Appears Unfavorable to the Government

A Major Threat to Monetary Policy

(Washington) The lawsuit over whether the abolition of gold clauses is illegal was debated in court today. The plaintiff, Norman, holds bonds of the Baltimore & Ohio Railroad, claiming that the bonds contain a clause for payment of principal and interest in gold, which should not be canceled according to the Constitution. Therefore, he requested that the railroad company be ordered to pay the debt interest of $22 in gold. Attorney General Cummings appeared in court on behalf of the government to defend the case and requested the court not to conclude the case until the government had submitted the required documents to the court. Chief Justice Hughes of the Supreme Court spoke about the government's free public bonds, which promised to be paid in a certain currency, and made a shocking statement, saying, "According to this public bond, where do you have any power or congressional power to change this promise?" This was addressed to Cummings. The verdict in this case is not expected to be released until around February. (Reuters Telegram, 12th)

(Washington) Government leaders today predict that the outcome of the gold case currently in litigation in the Supreme Court will be a major threat to the government's monetary plan. The Supreme Court is likely to issue a ruling unfavorable to the government today. (Guomin Telegram, 11th)

(Washington) Silver supporters in the House of Representatives are paying close attention to the Supreme Court's handling of the gold case. If the court's ruling is unfavorable to the government, then the method of recoining silver coins to devalue the US dollar will be more powerful. Representative White told a reporter from the Associated Press that he plans to propose a bimetallic standard and set the ratio of gold to silver at sixteen to one. If the court's ruling is unfavorable to the government, then recoining silver coins will be the only way to solve the currency problem. White also stated that raising the price of silver to $1.25 per ounce is necessary for economic recovery and that Senator Pittman's wartime silver purchase law has increased prices here. The situation in the East is better than ever before. He believes that the Treasury Department's policy towards China should consider the fact that China uses silver to purchase American goods. (Guomin Telegram, 11th)

Portugal Restores Parliamentary System 81

Lisbon Portugal has restored the parliamentary system that was abolished nine years ago. President Carmona presided over the opening ceremony of the new parliament today. The new parliament is composed of a National Assembly with ninety members and an upper house of a corporatist nature. Portugal has been manipulated by warlords since a military coup occurred in 1926, overthrowing the elected government and dissolving parliament. The new constitution was promulgated on March 19, 1933, stipulating the election of the National Assembly, whose representatives serve a term of four years. The president has the power to dissolve parliament. (Guomin Telegram, 11th)

Cessation of Anti-Chinese Sentiment in Mexico 118

Chinese Overseas Suffer Losses of Seventy Million Dollars

Change of President Leads to Return of Chinese Overseas to Mexico

(Mexico Correspondence) There are approximately over 60,000 Chinese overseas in Mexico. Those engaged in business were making substantial profits. Various businesses were mostly run by Chinese. However, since 1932, anti-Chinese sentiment in Mexico became increasingly intense. Chinese stores and farms in Sonora, Sinaloa, and Chiapas were almost completely looted by Mexicans. The losses in property and businesses of Chinese overseas reached sixty to seventy million dollars. More than two hundred people died, and many were deported. After the anti-Chinese sentiment erupted, the Kuomintang branches in various cities telegraphed the National Government to protect Chinese overseas. In the spring of 1933, the central government sent Huang Yunsou as envoy to Mexico. After Huang's arrival, he signed a commercial and protection treaty with Mexican President Cárdenas. Recently, the anti-Chinese sentiment in Mexico has begun to subside. Chinese overseas who had been deported are returning to Mexico from places like Taishan, Guangdong, to make a living. The current Mexican President Cárdenas cares for the overseas compatriots and is different from the former President Calles, who was cruel and tyrannical. (December 12th)

Postal Situation in the Northeast 119

Establishment of Yugu Transfer Bureau Facilitates Mail Transit

Mail in the South Manchurian Railway Zone Remains Under Old Regulations

Preparation for Scheduled Implementation of Remittances and Parcels Underway

(Beiping Correspondence) The postal service in the Northeast, which had been suspended for two and a half years, is now being restored under certain conditions. The Huitong Transfer Bureau, responsible for the transfer tasks, has established general and branch offices in Shanhaiguan and Gubeikou, which were officially established at 10 a.m. on the 10th. The Hebei and Beiping Postal Administration issued a circular on the 9th to all post offices under their jurisdiction, stating that starting from the 10th, they would officially receive and dispatch international mail to and from the Northeast and via Siberia. All international mail will be handled in accordance with international postal regulations. The postal service in the South Manchurian Railway Zone has always been subject to separate treaties and is collected by Japanese post offices. Afterwards, Chinese stamps must be affixed before they can be sent to inland areas. Those without stamps affixed will be penalized according to the underpayment method. After the resumption of postal service, the old regulations will remain in effect. Forged organization stamps and special stamps are not applicable. Mail from areas in the Northeast outside the Railway Zone for inland destinations must use special stamps. After arriving at Shanhaiguan and Gubeikou, the Huitong Transfer Bureau will handle the transfer. Any mail with forged organization stamps will be considered invalid and will be checked by the Transfer Bureau. Only after another type of stamp is affixed can it be delivered inland. For the convenience of settlement, all accounts will be settled by the Hebei Postal Administration and the Huitong Transfer Bureau, even though Shanhaiguan and Gubeikou belong to the Hebei and Beiping postal districts, respectively. The Beiping district and the Hebei district Postal Administration will then settle the accounts themselves through transfer methods. The post offices in Shanhaiguan and Gubeikou will retain their old names, while the post office on the other side in Shanhaiguan will be renamed the South Suizhong Post Office, and the Gubeikou side will be renamed the South Luoping Post Office, to avoid confusion. The special stamps have already been printed by the other party and are divided into four types: 2 cents, 4 cents, 8 cents, and 12 cents. The size is similar to our stamps. The Chinese price is printed in the upper left and right corners of the stamp, and the English price is printed in the lower two corners. Only the two characters "郵政" (Postal Service) are printed in the middle of the bottom. In terms of patterns, the 2-cent and 8-cent stamps have floral borders with a blue floral auspicious grain pattern in the middle. The 4-cent and 12-cent stamps have a Mount Changbai pattern. Postal service began on the 10th. Due to time constraints on that day, both parties only received letters, so Beiping had not yet received any incoming mail. Incoming and outgoing mail began on the 11th. The procedures for remittances and parcels are more complicated and require time to prepare. It is scheduled to be implemented on February 1st. Currently, the Huitong Transfer Bureau is rushing to print documents and preparing all procedures to ensure timely implementation. All accounts will also be directly settled by the Hebei Postal Administration and the Huitong Transfer Bureau. The handling and transfer by the Huitong Transfer Bureau is a trial. If there are difficulties, reforms will be made at any time to achieve perfection. The bureau charges commissions and does not collect other fees. Any profits or losses are unrelated to the Postal Administration. (10th)

Fang Juehui Arrives in Jinan to Mourn Zhang Weicun 120

Fang Temporarily Stays in Jinan to Assist in Directing the Arrest of the Murderer

(Jinan Correspondence) The central government attaches great importance to the assassination of Zhang Weicun and has repeatedly telegraphed Chairman Han to strictly arrest the murderer. On one hand, it dispatched Central Committee member Fang Juehui to Jinan to offer condolences and assist in directing the investigation of the case. Fang arrived in Jinan at 4:35 p.m. today (the 10th) on the Pingpu train No. 306. Provincial Chairman Han Fuju and various party and government officials welcomed him at the station. After getting off the train, Fang went to the Jiaoji Hotel for a temporary rest. At 5 p.m., Han hosted a banquet at the hotel, inviting provincial government advisors Han Duofeng, Zhang Liansheng, Ge Jinzhang, Councilor Yao Yijie, and Provincial Party Department Supervisory Committee member Zhang Zhuxi to accompany him. There was much discussion about the Zhang case during the banquet. The reporter interviewed Fang to inquire about everything. According to Fang, his mission here is to mourn Committee Member Zhang. Initially, due to matters in Beiping, he planned to go to Beiping, but after receiving a telegram from the central government, he came to Jinan first. The central government attaches great importance to this case and is determined to strictly arrest the murderer to uncover the truth. Matters concerning the aftermath and funeral expenses are not a problem. It is expected that the Central Standing Committee will raise them for discussion today (the 10th). He is determined to stay here for a few days. (10th)

Jianghan Engineering Bureau Sends Personnel 121

To Survey the Jiangxiang River Basin

Conducting In-depth Investigation of Main and Tributary Water Conservancy in Henan and Shaanxi

Chiang and Zhang Telegraph the Three Provinces' Authorities for Assistance

(Hankou Correspondence) The National Economic Commission's Jianghan Engineering Bureau, in order to survey the water conservancy, production, trade, and transportation conditions of the main and tributary basins of the Yangtze and Xiang Rivers, as the basis for planning and measuring the water conservancy, has specially organized two teams, the Yangtze River Survey Team and the Xiang River Survey Team. Chen Zhangguan was appointed as the captain of the Yangtze River team, Xu Shuping as the engineer, Li Eqi as the captain of the Xiang River team, and Sun Weibo and Yan Shouren as the engineers. The teams are divided into three groups, departing separately to conduct on-site surveys. The survey sites, in addition to the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River basin and Sichuan and Jiangxi, the Xiang River basin needs to be traced upstream, reaching dozens of counties in the southern parts of Henan and Shaanxi. Wherever the main and tributary rivers of the Hanshui River pass, the surveyors should be present. The source of the river is mostly located in the mountainous areas where the two provinces or two counties meet, which happens to be the area where the troops are currently encircling and suppressing bandits. Fearing that the local troops and county governments may refuse to provide protection when the survey team approaches the source of the river, which would prevent this important task of tracing the source from proceeding smoothly, Yang Silian, the director of the Jianghan Engineering Bureau, telegraphed Chairman Chiang and Vice Commander Zhang (Xueliang) for instructions. On the 10th, Chiang and Zhang jointly telegraphed the governments of Hubei, Henan, and Shaanxi, and the military authorities, strictly ordering the county governments and local troops to provide special protection and assistance to the team. It is reported that the survey team is scheduled to depart from Hankou within a few days. According to the person in charge of the Jianghan Bureau, in addition to surveying water conservancy, dikes, production, trade, and transportation conditions, other aspects such as labor, materials, education, etc. will also be investigated, as the basis for reorganizing and developing the Jiangxiang water conservancy. Therefore, the mission is extremely important. (10th)

Liu Puchen's Orphans Return to Shanxi from Beiping After His Death 122

Nan Guixin and Others Raise Funds for Liu's Aftermath

(Beiping Correspondence) Liu Puchen, who accompanied Huang Musong, the central government's envoy to pay respects to the Dalai Lama, passed away in Lhasa on the 7th of this month due to a stroke. Liu's relatives and friends here deeply regretted his passing. Liu never engaged in production, so his situation in recent years was not very prosperous. His orphans are currently studying in Beiping and Tianjin. After receiving the bad news, in addition to observing mourning rituals in Beiping the day before yesterday (the 8th), they also went to the residences of relatives and friends in Beiping, such as Nan Guixin, to report the funeral and request their assistance in handling the aftermath. After deliberations, Nan Guixin and others decided to discuss the matter in Taiyuan. It is said that the father of Yan Xishan, the director of the Taiyuan Pacification Office, has scheduled a memorial service at the Yan residence in Hebian Village on the 14th of this month. Renowned figures from Shanxi will attend the service, so it is planned to raise the matter for discussion at that time, as it will be easier with everyone's support. Nan and Liu's orphans will take the train to Taiyuan at 11 p.m. today (the 10th). The various situations are recorded as follows:

Liu Kongxiu, Liu's nephew, is studying at the Law School in Beiping. The reporter drove to visit him this afternoon (the 10th). Liu's daughter, Jinyun, had just arrived in Beiping from Tianjin and was packing her luggage with tears in her eyes. After expressing condolences, the reporter heard Miss Liu say, "My father was always in good health. He has been engaged in the revolution for decades, loves sports, and has no habits of smoking or drinking. This time, he was dispatched to accompany Minister Huang (Musong) to Tibet to pay respects to the Dalai Lama, which has been seven months. I never expected him to die in a foreign land, which we never anticipated. Before he left, my grandmother was still alive and strongly advised him not to travel far, but my father refused. Within two months of my father's departure, my grandmother passed away. Her coffin is still in the hall. We originally intended to bury her after my father returned, but I didn't expect such an accident to happen. According to the telegram from the Beijing side, the cause of my father's death was a stroke, perhaps due to the climate there. We are all young and have suffered a major disaster. Our minds are in chaos. We plan to return to our hometown tonight to handle everything according to my mother's instructions. However, my father was negligent in saving due to his engagement in the revolution, so our family is in a difficult situation. Thinking about the future, we are truly worried. After we return to our hometown and make some arrangements, we will transfer to Jinjing to pay respects to Minister Huang (Musong). As for the aftermath, we rely on the elders to plan for us." Miss Liu was unable to continue speaking at this point and burst into tears. Her grief was sincere and deeply moving. Liu's nephew, Liu Kongxiu, was also sobbing at his desk. After offering some consolation, the reporter left sadly.

After receiving the bad news from Lhasa, Liu's old friends in Beijing immediately sent a telegram to Beiping, reporting to Liu's son Kongzhang and nephew Yesiu, and offering warm condolences. The original telegram read, "Liu Kongxiu and Liu Kongzhang, Law School, Elephant Workshop Bridge, Mongolian Communications Office, Translated and Transferred: We have just received a telegram from Lhasa from Jiang to Yiyang (7th) stating that Old Man Pu suffered a stroke in the morning (6th) while riding a horse. After being treated by a doctor, he did not regain consciousness for a day and a night. He passed away at 5 a.m. on the morning of Yang (7th). Friends here are deeply saddened. We believe that you, brother, are sincere and will undoubtedly be overcome with grief. However, we believe that your father died for the country and has no regrets. We hope you will control your grief and take on major responsibilities. In addition to friends here jointly planning the aftermath, we are sending a telegram to express our condolences. If necessary, we will send another telegram to invite you, brother, to Beijing. Tang Kesan, Wu Heling, Ba Wenjun, Liu Funong, Xiong Yaowen, Yu (7th)." Liu was a native of Shenchi County, Shanxi, and was 53 years old. His wife is 40 years old and has one son and three daughters. The son, Kongzhang, is 21 years old and is studying at Beiping High School. The eldest daughter, Jinyun, is 25 years old and is studying at the Tianjin Municipal Hospital Nursing School. The second and third daughters live with their mother in their hometown. Liu has a cousin, named Kongxiu, who is 24 years old and is studying in the Department of Law at the Beiping Law School. Jiangsu Provincial Government Revises the Classification of Counties 123

(Zhenjiang News) The Jiangsu Provincial Government, based on the area, population, and wealth of each county, has revised the classification of counties, which was approved by the 716th meeting and will be implemented from the 24th year. The classification is as follows: First-class counties: Jiangning (should be classified as second-class, but is reclassified as first-class as an autonomous experimental county), Zhenjiang (should be classified as third-class, but is reclassified as first-class as the provincial capital), Wuxian, Changshu, Wujiang, Wujin, Wuxi, Nantong, Rugao, Yancheng, Funing, Jiangdu, Dongtai, Taixian, Tongshan.

Second-class counties: Danyang, Liyang, Songjiang, Nanhui, Kunshan, Yixing, Jiangyin, Taixing, Huaiyin (should be classified as third-class, but is reclassified as second-class as an important town north of the Yangtze River), Huaian, Lianshui, Xinghua, Taixian, Donghai (should be classified as third-class, but is reclassified as second-class as a key area for border defense and an important commercial port north of the Yangtze River), Guanyun (should be classified as third-class, but is reclassified as second-class as a future important commercial port).

Third-class counties: Jurong, Lishui, Gaochun, Jiangpu, Liuhe, Jintan, Yangzhong, Shanghai, Qingpu, Fengxian, Jinshan, Chuansha, Taicang, Jiading, Baoshan, Chongming, Haimen, Jingjiang, Siyang, Yizheng, Baoying, Fengxian, Peixian, Xiaoxian, Dangshan, Pixian, Suqian, Suining, Shuyang, Ganyu, Qidong. (December 12th)

Jiangxi Provincial Porcelain Exhibition 124

Aimed at Improving the Porcelain Industry

(Nanchang Correspondence) The porcelain of Jingdezhen, Jiangxi, is very famous in history and in the world. In the past, Europeans called porcelain "文那 (Wen Na)," and after the opening of maritime transport, the annual sales were always in the millions of dollars. Recently, foreign porcelain has stolen the show, coupled with natural and man-made disasters in the country and various influences, the porcelain industry has declined and fallen sharply. The number of Jingdezhen kiln owners who open kilns is less than half, and the number of unemployed workers is also increasing daily. All sectors of the country are paying close attention to this industry. Those who have gone to inspect one after another. All sectors of the province, in order to revitalize the porcelain industry and reverse the decline, in addition to selecting a large number of famous porcelain to participate in the Chicago Exposition last year, (4) also held a porcelain exhibition in Nanchang. Participants include the Jiangxi Porcelain Company, Jingdezhen Vocational School, and dozens of local Chinese stores in the city. The venue is in the Zhongshan Hall of the Yuzhang Park. There are slogans at the entrance saying, "Chinese people should use Chinese porcelain," "Chinese people should improve Chinese porcelain." The hall is winding and full of porcelain, all of which are products of Jingdezhen and local porcelain shops in the city, about tens of thousands of pieces, worth four to five hundred thousand dollars. The porcelain is priced lower than the market price. The opening ceremony was held at 10 am on the 7th. Hundreds of guests attended, chaired by Director Gong of the Construction Department, followed by the chairman of the Jiangxi Porcelain Improvement Society, Chen Changming, reporting on the preparations. He said, "We have seen that the porcelain industry, which has been glorious in the world for thousands of years, is declining. Therefore, we have gathered various porcelain merchants in Jingdezhen to form a porcelain industry improvement society. But if we want to improve, we must first examine its shortcomings. Therefore, we have decided to make a thorough review through the exhibition. This time, the collection of items, styles, calligraphy, and paintings should have everything. In order to revive Chinese porcelain and promote Chinese porcelain, we must not fail this exhibition." Finally, the chairman of the City Chamber of Commerce, Xu Ruifu, and others gave speeches, and then Director Gong's daughter cut the ribbon. After the ceremony, all sectors freely visited, and the audience was very enthusiastic. (January 7th)

Songjiang Refugees Gather to Cause Trouble in the Surrounding Villages 125

In recent times, groups of refugees from Henan and Jiangbei have been passing through the four villages of this county, begging for food. Often, the composition is complex, and there are times when they overstep the boundaries of their actions and gather to demand things. The villagers cannot bear the harassment. For example, the family of Cao Shaocun, a farmer in the 21st Tu of the Xinwu Ku Town, was broken into and harassed by Funing refugees the night before yesterday. They took the opportunity to rob him, stealing ten silver dollars and a fur coat. Fortunately, the neighbors rang the gong to warn, and the refugees fled. The villagers chased them in groups and intercepted three men and two women, who were taken to the town police station and then transferred to the county. They gave their names as Pan Shusong, Mao Jinyu, Pan Lianjin, Zhang Dengshi, and Pan Caishi. They did not admit to the robbery. The case was transferred to the county court for investigation. It is learned that Xia, the wife of the victim Cao Shaocun, was scalded in her lower body and is in great pain. The violence of the refugees is evident. It is also reported that 300 refugees from Henan arrived in Shihu Dang Town today (the 12th), men, women, old and young, gathered to cause trouble. After receiving a telegram from the town's merchants, the county government ordered the Public Security Bureau to send inspectors to the countryside and the 12th Security Brigade to send a squad of soldiers, and the Water Patrol Special Affairs Bureau to send two patrol boats to quell the situation.

Changshu Provincial Order Urgently Collects Land Tax 126

Zhao Lihua, the director of the Provincial Department of Finance, because the provincial treasury is in arrears and has no way to make up for it, found that the new and old arrears of land tax in this county reached 300,000 yuan. He then sent Commissioner Chen Naixun to Changshu to urge the collection. Unexpectedly, Commissioner Chen has been in Changshu for two months, but due to the poverty of the local area, the amount collected has not increased. Now, the Department of Finance believes that the amount of tax paid by this county is extremely short, and specially ordered Commissioner Chen to complete all old arrears from the 16th year to the 22nd year within this month, and must collect 10,000 yuan per day. Now, Commissioner Chen, after receiving the order, has joined the county government to strictly pursue the arrears from the people and officials and complete the payment as soon as possible.

Wuxi Continuous Rainfall and Declining Rice Prices 127

The weather in this county has been abnormal recently, with continuous rain for months, so the sale of rice in the market has been sluggish. In addition, the money supply is extremely tight, and many households have no way to pay. The storage of goods is abnormally crowded, resulting in a continuous decline in market prices. High-quality goods can still barely be maintained, but medium and low-quality goods cannot be hoarded, and no one is interested in them, so the decline is very sharp. Yesterday's market price of new brown japonica rice was 10 yuan and 8 cents to 8 yuan and 8 cents, new brown indica rice was 10 yuan and 4 cents to 8 yuan and 2 cents, new white japonica rice was 12 yuan to 10 yuan and 5 cents, and new white indica rice was 11 yuan and 7 cents to 8 yuan and 4 cents.

Verdict on the Xifeng Grain Merchant Giant Gambling Case 128

The Xifeng Grain Merchant in Ronghu Village, outside the North Gate of this county, was found to have been setting up a gambling table privately, gambling heavily day and night. On the winter solstice festival of the lunar calendar, the Inspectorate of the Public Security Bureau discovered it and went to arrest them. Seventy-five gamblers, including Feng Nankang, were arrested on the spot and taken to the bureau and transferred to the prosecutor's office of the local branch court for investigation. The investigation has now been completed, and a public prosecution has been filed with the criminal court. Yesterday, Judge Liu presided over the trial and announced the verdicts separately. Twelve people, including Feng Nankang, were fined 40 yuan each, and sixty-three people, including Wang Lanfen, were fined 30 yuan each as a warning. The total fine for the entire case was 2,370 yuan.

Robbery and Assault Case Occurs in the Sixth District of Changzhou 129

Zhou A'gen, a farmer in Qilin Township, the sixth district of Wu County, has 60 to 70 acres of land and is quite well-off. Unexpectedly, he was coveted by bandits and was searched once by bandits in November of last year. Forced by the bandits' power, he dared not report the case. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the 10th of this month at about 9:00 pm, more than a dozen bandits came again and searched arbitrarily. Zhu Gensheng, a neighbor, heard the noise and came out to see, but was caught by the bandits and beaten in the head and body, immediately falling to the ground. The bandits then left with the stolen goods. The Gensheng family saw that Gensheng's injuries were quite serious and sent him to the Wujin Hospital in the city for treatment on the 11th. The loss is still being checked.

The ninth redemption lottery for the Jiangsu Disaster Relief Public Bonds was held at the Chamber of Commerce Building on the afternoon of the 11th. The winning numbers are 133, 59, 81, and 00. Payment will be made at the Jiangsu branch of the Bank of Communications from January 31st.

Jiaxing Party Headquarters' Opinion on Resistance to Rent 131

A rent resistance incident occurred among tenant farmers in various townships of Jiaxing Xincheng. The landlords petitioned the county, ordering the arrest of the ringleaders. Who knew that the villagers tied up the police chief, and the situation escalated. Later, Yao Aqi and other 28 people were arrested and are currently detained in the Public Security Bureau. Since the occurrence of this case, the Party Headquarters has paid great attention to it and has now drafted a plan, which has been sent to the county for review. The plan is divided into (1) strictly investigate the instigators of the farmers' resistance to rent and pay attention to whether there is any background, (2) the detained farmers who resist rent should be allowed to be released on bail if they voluntarily notify their families to pay the rent in advance, (3) the rent payable should be reduced in accordance with the 25% rent reduction regulations and the provincial regulations on the number of years of famine, and the landlords should also consider reducing the rent to show compassion, (4) order the county farmers' association to quickly send personnel to the district farmers' association to persuade the farmers to pay the rent on time. It is reported that after the county government approved the letter, it has handled the various measures separately, in order to solve the problem as soon as possible, so as to avoid the escalation of the situation.

Two Deaths Caused by Trains and Cars in Hangzhou 132

Near Xucun Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, a farmer named Ye Chaoyong's son, Chunquan, was picking up coal on the railway tracks yesterday afternoon when the No. 61 express train from Shanghai passed by at high speed, knocking Chunquan off the tracks. He was seriously injured and sent to the Hangzhou City Station Hospital for treatment, but died. Also, near Qiaosi on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway, a large bus driven by driver Sun Qingyuan was returning to Hangzhou from Haining yesterday when a villager named Wang Jingquan was unable to avoid it in time and was crushed in the chest and abdomen, killing him on the spot. The driver was detained by the Public Security Bureau and sent to Hangzhou to be interrogated by the Hangzhou District Court.

Monk Executed by Firing Squad for Murdering for Money 133

Jianrong, a monk at Jingshan Temple in Yuhang, usually engaged in prostitution and gambling. Knowing that his fellow monk Liqin had accumulated surplus funds, he conceived the idea of murdering him for money. On April 23rd of last year, knowing that Liqin had gone out to collect debts and had not returned, he waited for him halfway with a gun. He met Liqin at the Banshan Pavilion and shot him dead at the Yubei Pavilion, dumping the body on the hillside and fleeing back to his original home in Chongde to hide. The abbot of the temple, Monk Shanlin, discovered this and reported it to the county court, which issued a warrant for Jianrong's arrest. He was sentenced to death. Jianrong refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the High Court, which sentenced him to death in accordance with the Regulations on the Punishment of Bandits. After being approved by the provincial government, the monk Jianrong was brought out at 9:00 am yesterday (the 12th), his identity was verified, and he was escorted to Qingchun Gate for execution by firing squad.

Freight Train Crushes Taoist to Death at Night 134

Mr. Liu, a Taoist priest from the San Yi Taoist Temple near Nanxing Bridge in Jianggan, was about 40 years old and from Shanxi. Recently, he suddenly suffered from a nervous illness. At about 3:00 am the day before yesterday, he wandered alone on the railway tracks at Nanxing Station. A night freight train on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway passed by, and Liu's head, hands, and feet were crushed by the freight train, which was a terrible sight. The railway bureau reported the case to the court, which sent Inspector Feng Yongnian to the scene for inspection before putting him in a coffin.

The Great Fire in Fenghua Bridge Town 136

The Fenghua Bridge Town pier of Tong Sheng Money Exchange caught fire at 3:00 am on the 10th due to the negligence of apprentice Lu Qihua when cooking snacks. The fire suddenly broke out and was extremely fierce and unapproachable. Fire brigades from inside and outside the city rushed to the scene and tried their best to put out the fire. Page 11

Local News

Various Foreign Firms Inform the Soybean and Grain Association of the Total Number of Foreign Rice Orders by Chinese Merchants 137

Total Estimated to Reach Over Five Million Bags

Supply Exceeds Demand, Rice Prices Decline Again

Dagon News reports that the Soybean and Grain Association in this city, due to the continuous arrival of foreign rice in China affecting the rural economy and the economy of the same industry, has sent letters to various foreign firms undertaking the rice trade, requesting them to investigate the actual numbers, and then warning the same industry to restrict orders. The various situations are recorded as follows:

Letter to Foreign Firms 138

Dear Sirs,

Upon investigation, this past year our country experienced a poor harvest of rice, leading to a shortage of rice grains. In Zhejiang Province, excluding the rice-rich areas of Wenzhou and Taizhou, it is estimated that there is a deficit of two million shi (石). Jiangsu Province faces a deficit of one million shi (石). Anhui Province has a slight surplus, while Hubei and Hunan Provinces are generally self-sufficient. Jiangxi Province is able to supply itself. According to these statistics, there is an approximate deficit of three million shi (石). Consequently, Chinese merchants are actively purchasing foreign rice to alleviate the situation. Current estimates suggest that foreign rice orders have reached five million bags, an astounding figure. If this estimate is indeed accurate, it will inevitably lead to a significant surplus, potentially causing drastic market price fluctuations in the future. Merchants will suffer losses, and foreign firms will also be adversely affected. Furthermore, the total value of five million bags of foreign rice would be around fifty million yuan. In this time of financial distress and economic decline across various sectors, difficulties in capital turnover are inevitable. Our association, considering these circumstances, is deeply concerned and intends to conduct a precise statistical analysis to prevent future problems. Therefore, we earnestly request that Your Firm provide, within three days, a detailed breakdown of the total amount of foreign rice ordered from Your Firm in Shanghai and Ningbo since last autumn, including: the amount that has already arrived; the amount that is en route but has not yet arrived; and the amount that has been ordered but has not yet been shipped. We kindly request that this information be provided accurately so that we can assess the situation and ensure safety. This matter concerns post-disaster management, so we hope that you will promptly respond accordingly. Sincerely, To [Name of Foreign Firm]. Enclosed is a survey form; please complete and return it to our Association.

Total Amount of Foreign Rice 139

Following the issuance of survey forms to various foreign firms in this port by the Bean, Rice and Grain Trade Association the day before yesterday, the Association received reports yesterday from Arnhold, Karberg & Co., Jebsen & Co., Sincere & Co., Gilman & Co., Jardine Matheson & Co., Carlowitz & Co., Jardine Engineering Corporation, Andersen, Meyer & Co., A. E. Ullmann & Co., and China Import & Export Lumber Co. The total amount ordered in Shanghai is 365,610 tons (each ton contains ten bags, totaling 3,656,100 bags, each bag weighing 180 jin by the market scale, equivalent to 1.2 shi by the market measure). The total amount ordered in Ningbo is 114,000 tons (totaling 1,114,000 bags). The firms handling the most orders are China Import & Export Lumber Co. and Jardine Engineering Corporation. However, eight foreign firms, including Dodwell & Co., Wing Tai, Heng Feng, Taisoo, Kam Lung, Cheung Mow, Paolung, and Taifung, have not yet submitted reports to the Association. In total, the actual amount of foreign rice ordered by local and foreign rice merchants, as well as financial institutions, must be over five million bags. All of these orders were placed between September and October of last year.

Continued Orders This Year 140

Rice merchants and financial institutions in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, as well as this city, have ordered foreign rice from Saigon, Siam, and other locations. Over two million bags arrived in Shanghai last year, and over three million bags with a later term will arrive at the end of January or early February of this year. A reporter from the Ta Kung Pao investigated the rice market yesterday and learned that since the stock market opened on January 3, rice merchants in this city have continued to order approximately 800,000 to 900,000 bags of foreign rice for later delivery in April and May.

Rice Prices Drop 141

The price of rice in this city, especially the best white rice, exceeded the price limit a few days ago. Secondary No. 3 rice and foreign Kexian rice also rose in price, causing unusual public panic. However, starting from January 9, prices suddenly fell, and have continued to drop in recent days. The current selling price for top-grade rice is 13 yuan, secondary-grade rice is 12.3 yuan and 11.23 yuan, South Bank secondary-grade rice is 10.23 yuan, and foreign Kexian rice is 10.08 to 10.09 yuan. Compared to last week's market prices, these represent a drop of more than half a yuan. According to rice industry leader Zhu Zixiang, who spoke to a reporter from the Ta Kung Pao, there are three reasons for this decline: (1) The Lunar New Year is approaching, leading to tighter credit; (2) Purchasing power is weak; (3) Foreign rice is arriving in Shanghai in a steady stream. According to the survey on the loss of harvest caused by last year's drought, approximately three million shi (石) needed to be supplemented. However, the amount ordered by the industry and financial institutions has exceeded this number. This year, the supply of rice will exceed demand, and rice prices will inevitably plummet, not only significantly affecting the industry but also causing substantial losses to farmers.

Late-Night Meeting 142

Since Sanpei (三北) insisted on including Mingxing (明興) in the alliance agreement, but the allocated profits would be reduced, while Taikoo, China Merchants and NingShao (寗紹) and others firmly disagreed and petitioned the Navigation Administration Bureau not to issue Mingxing (明興) navigation certificates, the two sides insisted fiercely. On the evening of the day before yesterday, the director of the Navigation Administration Bureau, Peng Hu (彭瑚), summoned Liu Hongsheng (劉鴻生) of China Merchants, Yu Qiaqing (虞洽卿) of Sanpei (三北), and Yuan Ludeng (袁履登) of NingShao (寗紹), etc., to the Navigation Administration Bureau for an emergency meeting. Director Peng (彭) persuaded both parties to make concessions to each other. The meeting lasted for five hours. The discussion was very secretive, and a solution was not reached until late at night.

Settlement Plan 143

Although the resolution cannot be made public, according to the reporter's investigation, when discussing the opposition of the three companies to the Mingxing (明興) wheel joining the Shanghai-Ningbo line, Liu Hongsheng (劉鴻生) of China Merchants proposed that Sanpei (三北) lease Mingxing (明興) to China Merchants, which Sanpei (三北) also agreed to, but the issue of management rights was not resolved, so the discussion was changed to the handling of Mingxing (明興) wheel. As a result, roughly, "the Shanghai-Ningbo four companies stipulate that each company should send only one ship for navigation, and no more ships should be added." The company sent ships to replace them, and the general situation is recorded as follows:

Collision of Japanese Ship 144

The Xin Shengjing (新盛京) wheel is a regular passenger ship on the North China Sea route. Recently, due to the silting of the Baihe River in Tianjin, most ships to Tianjin only go to Tanggu. After the ship arrives in Tanggu, passengers and cargo are transferred to Tianjin, and the ship stays at the Tanggu wharf to load cargo bound for the south. It was originally scheduled to leave Tanggu on the 11th. On the 10th, when loading cargo, a Japanese merchant ship suddenly arrived in Tanggu. Due to careless navigation, it crashed into the Xin Shengjing (新盛京) wheel. Xin Shengjing (新盛京) was at anchor, and when the ship crashed into it that day, it could not avoid the collision, and was damaged. The outer hull of the ship was damaged. The detailed damage situation was not described in detail in the Shanghai telegraph, so it is still impossible to know the truth. It will only be clear after the ship arrives in Shanghai. Fortunately, the engine room was not affected, so it was still able to depart from Tanggu and come to Shanghai.

Suspension for Repairs 145

Reporters from this newspaper inquired at the company, and it was said that the Xin Shengjing (新盛京) wheel was severely damaged in the collision with the Japanese ship this time. The company has sent a telegram to Tianjin to inquire, and has decided to unload the cargo and suspend operations after the ship returns to Shanghai, and to carry out major repairs in the factory. As for the sailings that the Xin Shengjing (新盛京) wheel should have made, the company will deploy the Daming (大名) wheel to replace it.

Negotiations Underway 146

The name of the Japanese ship that caused the accident has now been determined by the Taikoo branch in Tanggu, as well as the shipowner's company. The report was made to the Tianjin Customs on the spot, and a surveyor was invited to inspect the damage to the ship in order to provide a basis for negotiations and claims.

Postal Administration to Move to Beijing This Month 147

Savings and Remittances Administration Also Scheduled to Move Next Month

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai Sichuan Road Bridge Postal Administration and the Postal Savings and Remittances Administration, after receiving orders from the Ministry of Communications to move to Beijing, the Postal Administration has begun to move in batches, and the entire move can be completed by the 20th of this month. As for the Postal Savings and Remittances Administration, it was originally scheduled to start moving next month, but due to practical difficulties, it may not be able to complete the move on schedule. The following is a statement from Xu Baiyuan, Deputy Director of the Savings and Remittances Administration:

The General Administration Moves to Beijing 148

Mr. Xu told a reporter from the Central News Agency that the Ministry of Communications originally set February 10 as the date for the relocation of the Administration to Nanjing, but the initial plan was to allocate a portion of the buildings built by the Postal Administration for use. Now, because these buildings have all been allocated for other uses, and the internal organization and scale of the Administration are more complex, there is no space available for the Administration to use. The Administration is now planning to find suitable buildings in Beijing to serve as the Administration's office, but it has not yet been found, so the date of the move is difficult to determine before it is found. If suitable buildings can be found in the shortest possible time, the Administration can move to the capital for office within February.

Expansion of the Shanghai Bureau 149

Mr. Xu also told reporters that after the Administration moves to Beijing, the organization of the Shanghai Bureau will be slightly expanded compared to the current organization. In the past, the Shanghai Bureau and the Administration worked in the same place. The Ministry of Communications ordered that the original work of the Shanghai Bureau be transferred to the General Administration for management in order to save expenses. However, the savings and remittances work in the Shanghai area is quite heavy, so after the Administration moves to Beijing, the Shanghai Bureau must restore its original state in fact.

Rural Investment 150

When asked about the Administration's investment in rural areas, he replied that the Administration is happy to invest in rural areas, but the Administration's organization is slightly different from that of banks. At present, various banks have set up branches in the interior to handle rural investment, which is more convenient. The Administration mostly entrusts postal bureaus in the interior to handle savings and remittances, which is already extremely busy. There is no time to take care of investment matters. If the Administration establishes an investment management agency in the interior, it will also be beyond its economic capacity. Therefore, the Administration's investment in rural areas will cooperate with banks in the future, but this matter is still under planning, and will only proceed after the planning is completed.

Match Industry Tries to Reverse Business Decline 152

According to the Central News Agency, the business of domestic matches has been sluggish recently. Manufacturers from various provinces have held meetings in Shanghai to jointly seek relief. It has been decided that all factories in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Hubei, and Anhui provinces will proceed with merger procedures to avert the crisis. Reporters from the Central News Agency, because the match factory is one of our country's industries, and is especially necessary for the daily use of the general public, and is very important to people's livelihood, visited Mr. Gao Songfu, a member of the National Match Industry Federation, yesterday to inquire about the situation of the match industry. According to Mr. Gao, our country's match factories have produced both sulfide phosphorus and safety matches. In North China, such as the provinces of Shandong, Henan, Hebei, Beijing, Suiyuan, Gansu, and Shanxi, red-headed sulfide phosphorus matches are mainly sold. In South China, such as the provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, Guangdong, Guangxi, Fujian, Sichuan, Yunnan, etc., black-headed safety matches are mainly sold. However, the cost of sulfide phosphorus matches is about one-third lower than that of safety matches. In recent years, the production of sulfide phosphorus matches has been greatly excessive, so they have expanded their sales force in the northern part of Jiangsu, Anhui, and Hubei provinces. The original sales area of safety matches is therefore easily squeezed and changed. Also, considering the demand for matches in the provinces of Austria, Guizhou, Fujian, Sichuan, and Yunnan, it has mostly been supplied by manufacturers in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. In recent years, it has also been affected by the encroachment of foreign goods and the crackdown on provincial control. The original sales area of safety matches has not only been squeezed and changed, but also suddenly shrunk, resulting in a situation of overproduction, leading to a gradual and tragic drop in market prices, which has become more and more severe. The sluggishness of its business is unprecedented in the past years. According to investigations, the safety matches produced by manufacturers in the six provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi are about 270,000 cases per year, while the demand for safety matches by the people of the six provinces is about 210,000 cases per year. According to this, the number of safety matches that are overproduced each year is about 60,000 cases. This is still in terms of the production volume of manufacturers in the six provinces. If each factory is calculated to produce as much as possible, the annual production of safety matches is about 500,000 cases, which can exceed the actual sales volume by more than double. If the government is not requested to restrict the establishment of factories, and the industry does not restrain production, then the match industry will never be optimistic. Therefore, manufacturers from various provinces have risen up to find ways to seek relief. In addition to requesting the government to limit the establishment of new factories to provide assistance, they have also advocated mergers and joint operations, flat-price sales, and triangular agreements to limit production and other methods. Currently, He Shichang, Sun Runzhai, and Xi Jianqing of the match industry are leading manufacturers in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Hubei to organize the Preparatory Office for the Merger of Eight Factories of the Great China Match Company, located in the China Merchants Building on Edward Road, Shanghai. The Minsheng Match Factory in Suzhou has heard of this and has also requested to join. In the future, after the Guangming Match Factory in Wenzhou participates, it will become a company merged by ten factories, and will implement various plans such as agreement and joint operations. The decline of the domestic match industry may be saved.

Cotton Control Association Announces Bumper Cotton Harvest in Shaanxi Province Last Year 159

Totaling Over 1,004,000 Dan

According to the Ta Kung Pao, the National Economic Commission's Cotton Control Association released a message yesterday stating that since the establishment of the Cotton Production Improvement Institute in Xi'an last April, the total area of cotton in Shaanxi Province last year was more than 700,000 mu, an increase of 80% compared to the previous year, with a total harvest of more than 1,004,000 dan of cotton, an increase of 95% compared to the previous year. 17 cotton production cooperatives have been established, with more than 16,000 members. In terms of marketing, due to the benefits of low-interest loans and increased ginning and baling facilities, the cost per dan of cotton can be reduced by more than 5 yuan. Furthermore, by improving the quality of goods and reducing moisture content, each dan can be sold for more than 4 yuan. In total, farmers can directly increase their income by 10 yuan per dan of seed cotton. The benefits of improved seeds and increased yields are not yet included.
