Mr. Science Performs Magic 275

— He Gongchao

Celebrating Children's Year

Not long after the New Year of the Republic of China in 1935, Mr. Science was on stage again. In his hand, he held a piece of white paper and a new calligraphy brush that had never been used. His assistant also held three small bottles, one with alkaline water, one with vinegar, and one with litmus solution.

As soon as he took the stage, he bowed to the children below and said:

"This year is 'Children's Year,' and I congratulate you all. I hope that starting this year, your bodies will become stronger and stronger, and your knowledge will improve day by day. I hope you will be even more interested in studying scientific knowledge. I hope that in the New Year of 1936, your bodies and knowledge will be much better than they are now. Now, let's perform a magic trick":

He spread the white paper on the table, dipped the new brush in the alkaline water bottle, picked up the brush and wrote the words "Celebrating" on the white paper. After it dried, he dipped some vinegar and continued to write the three words "Children's Year". After a while, these five words completely disappeared, leaving no trace. It still looked like a piece of white paper.

He took out some litmus solution, added a little clear water, and held a mouthful. He called his assistant to pick up the white paper and sprayed the water from his mouth directly onto the paper. Immediately, the blue words "Celebrating" appeared on the white paper, and the red words "Children's Year" appeared.

Celebrating Children's Year 276

How fun! So there was a round of applause from below...

"Do you know why this happens? It turns out that litmus solution turns blue when it comes into contact with alkaline substances, and it turns red when it comes into contact with acidic substances. Alkali is a type of alkaline substance, and vinegar is a type of acidic substance. Therefore, writing words on paper with alkali water and vinegar will reveal red and blue strokes.

"Is your school going to have a fair? Why don't you perform this trick for everyone - you can write a few words or draw a picture.

"Where can you buy alkali and vinegar? You can just ask your mother or sister. Litmus solution can be bought at the scientific instrument store."

Experiment tools: one new brush, one piece of white paper.

Chemicals: alkali, vinegar, litmus solution.

A Cake Made by Over a Thousand People 277

— Jun Peng

Last Sunday, I went to eat at a relative's house, and during the meal, I heard something very strange, which was "a cake made by over a thousand people."

That relative said to his son, Fuyue, "We will eat cake in a while. This cake was made by over a thousand people." Fuyue showed a surprised look and said, "Father! This cake must be made by over a thousand people, it must be taller than that house!" I also found it very strange. After a while, the cake actually came, but it was not particularly tall. It was a very ordinary fruit cake. Fuyue smiled and said, "Is this it? The cake you just mentioned," the father said, "That's right!" Fuyue continued, "Didn't you say it was made by over a thousand people?" We all ate a piece, and the father said with a smile, "Now, go to your bag and get the slate and slate pencil and help me calculate the workers who made this cake!"

The father said, "To make cake, you must first grind flour. Flour is made from rice, and rice is hulled from grains. The fruits of rice are grains, which farmers grow. Don't you think there are already many people? Plowing requires plows, and plows require blacksmiths and carpenters. Grinding flour requires mills, and mills require stonemasons. Aren't there many more people here? The fruit is transported from afar. There are fruit growers and fruit sellers. Adding them up, there must be many more people. At the same time, steaming the cake requires burning coal. Miners mine the coal, and then people who make iron pots make the pots. And when steaming the cake, you need to use cloth to line the bottom, so there are cotton growers and textile workers and people who make weaving machines. I don't know how many more people need to be added!" When the father said this, his very smart son, Fuyue, said, "Okay, okay, Father, I have already counted over a thousand people." Little friends! Do you believe that this cake really requires over a thousand people to make? We must know that the cake we ate was not easy to come by!

Several Interesting Numbers in the Human Body 278

— Chang Su

The human body contains a total of 210 bones, of which the skull bones account for 28, the trunk bones account for 52, and the limb bones account for 130. Children have even more than this number, an increase of nine, because some bones will fuse together in adulthood.

The total length of the large and small intestines is about 25 feet, with the small intestine accounting for four-fifths and the large intestine only about five feet. The teeth of an adult total 32, with incisors (commonly known as front teeth) totaling eight, canines (commonly known as canine teeth) totaling four, premolars totaling eight, and molars totaling twelve. As for children's milk teeth, they are all replaced by the age of seven or eight, totaling 20.

When a man takes a deep breath, the amount of air that enters and exits is about 3,000 cubic centimeters, and during normal breathing, it is about 500 cubic centimeters. The amount of breathing for ordinary women is less than that for men.

The amount of blood pumped out by the heart in a normal state is about two gallons per minute (each gallon equals 3.78 liters), and more than 120 gallons per hour. The speed at which blood flows in the blood vessels is two feet per second, about seven miles per hour, and about 168 miles per day. The heart beats an average of 73 times per minute and about 4,320 times per hour. These numbers are amazing!

Gramophone 279

— Huosheng

Little friends, isn't it fun to turn on the gramophone when we are free? But you have to know how hard the person who invented the gramophone worked to achieve today's success!

Everyone knows that the gramophone was also invented by Edison. When he first invented it, it was very incomplete. His workers heard him say that a machine he had prepared could make human voices, and they thought that the old man was deliberately joking with him. No one believed him. Who knew that Edison actually spent ten years of work to make the gramophone, which everyone did not believe in, completely perfect and contribute it to the world. Once, he did not sleep for five days and nights in a row to improve the gramophone, working in one breath!

From this, it can be seen that there is no such thing as "gain without effort" in the world!

Children's Science Lecture: The Wonders of Plant Leaves 280

— Lin Yin

Have you heard your teacher say that plants breathe? You may be skeptical. Only animals have lungs or gills for respiration, so can plants also have lungs or gills? No, plant respiration is due to leaves, the chloroplasts of the leaves. If you don't believe me, we can try an experiment to prove it. Take the leaves of a plant and put them in a glass, and then cover them with a paper cover to prevent the inflow of outside air. After two or three hours, if you put a paper twist lit with fire into the glass, the fire will immediately go out. (Figure 1) This makes it clear that the leaves of the plant absorb the oxygen in the glass, and the glass is full of carbon dioxide, so the fire of the paper twist can no longer burn.

We know that the important nutrients of plants are water. When a plant is about to wither, just water it and it will revive. When there is too much water, it is evaporated by the leaves. The absorption and evaporation of plants is the same as human respiration. Let's take the glass and paper cover that we just used and try the evaporation of the leaves again. Fill the glass with water, make a small hole in the paper cover, and insert a leaf of the plant into the hole in the paper cover, letting the petiole soak in the water. Then take another glass that has been wiped very dry and cover it below (Figure 2). After ten minutes, uncover the glass and look. The glass that was just wiped dry is now moist, as if someone has breathed on it. Do you understand where the moisture in the glass comes from? I think, smart little friends! You will definitely answer that this is the water that the leaves absorbed from below the paper cover and evaporated.

The most wonderful thing about plant leaves is that they can prevent enemies, just like animals have claws and teeth for self-defense. The leaves of cacti that we usually see are like thorns, and the edges of holly leaves are sharp spines (Figure 3). If you touch them with your hand, you will feel pain, so you can avoid being harmed by others. On the other hand, they are responsible for protecting, helping new shoots emerge from the solid ground, like bamboo shoots. Leaves in plants are really like the role of our human limbs. Do you think they are so smart!

The Adventures of Sinbad the Sailor (Part 2) 281

— Xin Qing

I remained there, struggling for my life. I clung to that piece of wood for a day and a night, so I didn't sink. I thought I only had a short time to live, but the next day a good wind drove me to the shore of a small island. I was extremely exhausted from lack of food.

The rocks on this coast were very steep. If it weren't for the roots of the trees and other plants that gave me a foothold, I would never have had the chance to climb up and reach a place where the waves couldn't reach.

I ate some herbs that I found and drank some water from a clean and fresh spring. Then I set off to see what I could find.

Not far from where I was, I saw a horse, and I walked over to it. The horse was a fine animal, and I stood there looking at it for a long time.

After a while, I heard a voice, and a man was standing in front of me. He said, "Who are you?"

After I told him my miserable situation, he took me to a cave. I saw many more people there. They gave me food and drink, which I enjoyed very much. They told me that they were servants of King Melechi of the island. I found that this was a good opportunity to go with them to the town, which was some distance away.

If it weren't for these people, I would have died. Without their help, I would not have found my way to the inhabited part of the island, and those servants only came to this place once a year.

The next day we set off for the capital of the island. When we arrived, they took me to see their king. He said, "Who are you? And how did you get here?"

After I told him, he ordered his men to provide me with everything I needed in terms of clothing, food, and money.

The town where I now live is a port on the coast. Ships from all over the world can be seen here.

As the days passed, I spent a lot of time near the sea, because I thought maybe a ship from my hometown would come, or I could hear news of Baghdad, or find a small boat to take me back.

King Melechi has an island called Ganser Island. I once went to this island and saw very large fish there, some of which were over a hundred feet long. I also saw some fish that were less than two feet long, and their heads looked like owls.

One day a large ship came in. As soon as the ship was moored, the sailors began to take all the cargo out of the hold.

I stood aside watching them work, thinking how happy I would be, when I saw several packages with my own name on them. These goods were exactly what I had brought with me when I set out from Basra.

I told the captain that these things were mine. At first, he would not let me take them, saying that Sinbad was dead and that I must be an imposter.

He said, "When people look at you, they always think you are a good and honest person. But I saw Sinbad die. When that big fish swam, it took him straight to the depths of the sea. So how could you be Sinbad? I think everything you say is false."

I said, "If you are willing to listen to me carefully, I think I can prove it to you. I am Sinbad, whom you think you saw sink to the bottom of the sea."

So I told him everything that had happened! How I was thrown ashore by the waves and met the king's servants, who took me to the court.

Commercial News

Domestic Financial and Foreign Exchange Markets Remain Flat; No External Assistance for Speculative Funds 282

Sharp rise followed by a steep fall... Retreats by two yuan

Since the gold market rebounded the previous day, the overseas silver market contracted yesterday. The market opened rather firm, but the exchange rate market failed to tighten in unison. Major players took advantage of the high prices to collectively supply the market, gradually moving downstream. Although the Central Bank repeatedly opened spot bids, which helped to maintain the level, selling pressure ultimately prevailed, and prices fell again. The market started firm in the morning but weakened later in the day, resulting in an overall decline. The general trend was mediocre. It was observed that the overseas silver market fell in both the UK and the US at the beginning of the morning, and forward silver prices also contracted. The exchange rate continued to fall, while the price of London gold rose by five pence. Pre-market trading opened, immediately rising to over 67 yuan. The Central Bank's listed prices were announced, with the pound unchanged and the US dollar contracting by 0.0625. New York Stock Market Suffers Uniform Decline 287

Xin Feng Foreign Firm reports that the New York stock market suffered a disastrous decline yesterday (the 11th). Speculators, fearing that the Supreme Court would uphold the gold clause, sold off stocks and commodities and purchased bonds with gold clause provisions. Traders bought US dollars in the foreign exchange market, causing the US dollar to rise. US government bonds, which had been sluggish since August of last year, suddenly saw lively trading yesterday as traders sold off bonds without gold clause provisions and exchanged them for those with gold clause provisions. Railway companies with large gold clause debts saw particularly sharp declines in their stocks and bonds. Brokers reported that there are currently a large number of orders to sell at limit prices, indicating that speculators are deeply concerned that the Supreme Court's decision will be unfavorable to the government. The stock market's decline was quite severe, and Chicago wheat also fell due to the uncertain outcome of the gold clause, triggering a large-scale sell-off. US Cotton Awaits New Developments 297

A New York telegram dated January 11 reports on the cotton market situation for the week: The cotton market situation this week is still stable. After the bullish trend began, the South sold slightly more, while the bearish trend was curbed by purchases from foreign and domestic firms. Speculators are awaiting new developments in Washington, especially paying attention to the limits of the Bankhead Act and the government's policy of releasing cotton bonds in 1935, so interest is currently not strong. General commerce is becoming more optimistic, but buyers are unwilling to store more cotton, as the number of sales from the South is not small, and at current prices, it is enough to satisfy current demand. The price difference between cotton in New York and Liverpool is increasing, and the claim that foreign cotton that can compete with US cotton has a more firm market price is becoming more credible. Thus, when prices here fall slightly, merchants related to foreign countries continue to purchase. The Department of Agriculture estimates that the world production of various types of cotton in 1934 was 26 million bales, each weighing 478 pounds, a decrease of 3.1 million bales compared to the previous year. The cotton cloth market situation this week is calm and firm.

Because the factory booked a ship of Argentine wheat at a price of 4.875 yuan, the market saw brisk selling, and the market continued to fall. According to industry observers, the market should not be too weak as domestic consumption can continue. However, after the continued booking of imported wheat and the increase in capital, it may be difficult to see a strong recovery. As a result, the current month fell by 0.2 fen, February fell by 0.175 fen, March fell by 0.225 fen, April and May fell by 0.2 fen, and June fell by 0.275 fen.

Wheat Market Had Some Short Covering 299

Forward contracts showed a loosening trend

Yesterday's wheat market was generally flat after the opening in the morning. The prices for imported wheat in Chicago fell by about 5-7 cents, and in Canada by about 1-2 cents. Trading in the current month was very light when prices were opened, and market sentiment was calm. Although forward contracts were affected by the small price of imported wheat, selling was not smooth, and prices hovered. When the market opened in the afternoon, prices were slightly firmer in the current month due to slight short covering. In the forward months, market sentiment was slightly weaker due to news of continued bookings of imported wheat. As a result, the current month was up by 0.3 fen, March was down by 0.2 fen, and there was no change in the rest. The spot wheat market was still good, and arrivals were not abundant, so prices remained stable. Shandong Guidemai opened at 4.034 yuan, Yaowanmai at 4.01 yuan, and Xinpumai at 4.02 yuan, totaling 8,000 bags, which was handled by Fuxin.

Chicago Wheat and Corn were weak and the external markets were low, leading to the exposure of limit-down sell orders.

He Xia Rice Arrivals are Scarce and Turning Good 300

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the sources from various gangs were obstructed by heavy fog, and then turned scarce again. Only the 20th arrived (a total of more than 4,000 shi). Market sentiment was restored by the cloudy and rainy weather, and the late rice also had Qingdao gangs continuing to handle 400-500 bags, so the market rebounded by several fen. Early rice also saw a slight improvement. Only the price of Su Tong japonica rice remained stable as supply and demand were balanced. Due to the lack of goods and smooth sales, Du Jian saw a prominent increase. Foreign glutinous rice continued to be out of the market, while Yinbianyuan's path was not broad, and the market was uniquely weak.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, the arrivals at the wharf were around the 20th. Due to the continued rain, the sales of various types were sluggish, and the market shape has been declining recently. Due to high costs, customers were unwilling to release their positions. The market price of white japonica special goods stood firm. High-grade prices fell by 0.1-0.2 yuan. Other than Bo Dao Xiaojiao, Bian Yuan Xiaojin Jiao, and the remaining goods barely stood firm.

Foreign Rice Frequently Falls, Seems to Have Stabilized 301

Customer Xian arrivals and inventories are low

Yesterday's foreign rice market continued the bearish trend of the previous day, and the market and market sentiment declined again. No one asked about futures, new transactions stopped, and sales inquiries continued. However, importers were watching, and the whole market only opened Saigon rice for immediate shipment of 200 tons, with the price only at 4.62 yuan, and the market shape was still not stable. Spot foreign rice was very active in the mainland yesterday, with 3,100 bags going to the mainland, all of which were secondary machine rice and broken rice. 1,200 bags of machine rice went to this street, and prices were generally 0.1-0.15 yuan lower than the previous market. Customer Xian was very active in this street yesterday due to the high production price and low arrivals and inventories. The market seemed to have stabilized. Yesterday, a total of 2,500 bags of Xiang rice and 430 bags of Shashi brown rice were opened. In addition to 400 bags of machine yuan going to Tianjin and 750 bags of broken brown rice going to the mainland, all were taken in by this street.

Shantou Gang Purchases Forward Soybean Cake 302

Recently, the sales of soybean cake have continued, so the market price has fallen and rebounded. Yesterday, the Shantou gang began to purchase spot soybean cake for forward delivery. It is estimated that the delivery price for February for four-brand cake is 1.44 yuan. Changde Factory sold 5,000 pieces, Da You Factory 10,000 pieces, Sui Feng Factory 10,000 pieces, and Da De Xin Factory 15,000 pieces. The market sentiment is tight, and the Dalian telegram continued to rise, so the market is temporarily viewed as stable. The market situation for yellow soybeans is that the sales of Hankou goods are slow, and they are still weak. The sales of Guidemai soybean factory on the Longhai Railway are still connected, and the bottom accumulation is not thick, so the market remains stable.

Wheat Bran Foreign Banks Remain Unmoved for a Month 303

The wheat bran market has been silent for days, because foreign banks have been unmoved for nearly a month. On the mainland side, sales have turned sluggish due to the settlement of accounts and tight credit. Market sentiment is uniformly weak, and each stall's asking price opens at 2.66 yuan, or even 2.65 yuan. After this, if imported wheat remains quiet, or due to credit relations, it will present a fixed situation.

Sugar Market Sugar Industry Cooperative First Batch of Raw Sugar White Auctions 304

The price is 2.525 Dutch currency

Yesterday's sugar market saw raw sugar white showing a slight soft trend, slightly declining. The quoted price of domestically produced green sugar remained firm and continued to rise. The association divided 24 raw sugar white, spot ordinary 18.95 yuan, and this stack of goods 19.05 yuan, all down 5 fen. 11,000 bags of 24 raw sugar white were auctioned by the Sugar Industry Cooperative, of which 8,300 bags are expected to arrive on the 28th of this month, and 2,700 bags in February. The price is 2.525 Dutch currency, 99 deduction. The current price of ordinary 89 raw red Dutch sugar is 13.9 yuan. There are no changes in Taikoo Sugar and our factory's white sugar. Chaozhou Gang continued to open a batch of Chaoqing sugar, totaling nearly 2,000 bags. Ti Zhuang Qing is 11 yuan with no up or down, Huanggang Qing is 10.7-10.8 yuan, Bannan Qing is 10.04-10.05 yuan, and Longgang Qing is 10.02 yuan, with slight increases. Guang Gang opened more than 100 bags of Qingyuan Pian Qing, with a higher price of 10.3 yuan.

North and South Goods, Hunan Lotus Seeds Sales in Mainland Slightly Move 305

Prices have turned around

Recently, Hunan lotus seeds have gradually seen increased sales in Hangzhou, Shaoxing, and other places, and the market trend has been slightly rebounding. The purchase price in Hankou is also very stable, with higher prices at 28 yuan, followed by 26 yuan. Market prices in the production area are relatively flat, and the Shanghai market is slightly higher than before. Top Xiangtan lotus seeds are selling for 33 yuan, and the rest are reduced accordingly. White lotus seeds are in short supply, and the current market price is 42 yuan, which is extremely firm.

Metals, Many Metal Orders Were Made 306

Yesterday, there was less metal trading due to the rain, so there were not many openings for various goods. However, overseas order trading flourished, so 2,000 boxes of American tinplate were ordered yesterday, each box at 4.4 gold yuan, up 5 fen, made by Yongxing Foreign Firm. 500 bundles of 24-28 gauge plain sheet iron were also made, with the price pulled to 13 pounds, down 2 shillings and 6 pence from before. Tinplate tiles of 24-28 gauge were also made, and it was heard that 600 bundles were traded, with the price at 12.5 pounds per ton. In addition, it was heard that new foreign silver dollars such as brass were also made, but the market has not changed.

Bamboo Shoot Factories Purchase Tinplate 307

Ningbo bamboo shoot factories all sent letters yesterday to purchase tinplate. Although not many transactions were made, there were many embellishments for various colors. It was heard that 400-500 boxes of tinplate were thrown away, with prices such as 33.5 yuan for 100-pound German goods, and 35 yuan for US goods. 31.5 yuan for 90-pound German goods, and 33 yuan for US goods (double-linked above). If single-linked, 90-pound German goods open at 16 yuan, US goods at 16.25 yuan, 100-pound German goods at 16.75 yuan, and US goods at 17.25 yuan. 300-pound Heshi iron is 29 yuan.

Oil Market Hankou Tung Oil Arrivals are Very Scarce 308

Since the beginning of the year, Bai Tong oil has seen Hankou deliver goods to foreign firms for days, mostly forward oil sold previously. As the source is not prosperous, all arrivals are used to offset futures, so current deliveries are very scarce, and foreign firms have few transactions. The price is still 31 yuan per dan, and they do not dare to sell too much because there is no delivery. Foreign firms have had a good appetite recently, but firms want to increase the price, intending to be 32 yuan, and it is okay to throw some, but foreign firms are unwilling to do much, so there are no transactions. Firms have been opening deliveries to customers for days, estimating Xiangtong to be 26 yuan plus change, Tianjin goods to be 25.7-25.8 yuan, and Nanzhi to be around 25 yuan, all according to customer rules, totaling 1,600-1,700 dan. Considering the scarcity of the source, it is feared that the market will be difficult to hope for. Most of the Zhejiang Tung oil produced this year is insufficient, also due to age, so those that can meet the standards and be delivered to foreign banks generally require more than 26 yuan per stone, and insufficient goods are around 25.2-25.4 yuan.

Women's Corner

Meng Jiangnu's Reincarnation 327

— Ying Shen

Whether Meng Jiangnu actually existed in history is still a question, but the fact that Qin Shi Huang built the Great Wall is probably reliable. Qin Shi Huang forced people into corvée labor, and the people sacrificed under his tyranny were far more than just Meng Jiangnu's husband (assuming she existed). The number of widows created by this tyranny was far more than just Meng Jiangnu. At that time, needless to say, many tragedies occurred, so why is it that only Meng Jiangnu became famous? This is a bit strange. We can see from Meng Jiangnu's ballads that she is mainly celebrated as a chaste woman, and it can even be said that she is famous for her good crying; originally, such a person was not worthy of "immortality," but for thousands of years, people have been singing her name. Therefore, we have the right to have such doubts; the so-called Meng Jiangnu is a character shaped by later rulers according to their own models. Because the legendary Meng Jiangnu does not contain any danger to the ruling class, on the contrary, she is an ideal figure that suits the tastes of the rulers. Instead, she was praised by feudal society.

But now Meng Jiangnu has actually been reincarnated! The "Jinan Express" tells us that a "Jinan Meng Jiangnu" has come to Jinan (in fact, she came from Shaanxi, so she should be called Shaanxi Meng Jiangnu, but the Jinan reporter insisted on recognizing her as a fellow villager and taking it as an honor!) Han Guiqing, "traveled thousands of miles to find her husband, determined not to give up." The reporter only "recorded the outline of her deeds on the left," which is tens of thousands of words! The tone is full of praise. Allow me to drop a sentence, "This is not accidental." The conditions for producing this kind of Meng Jiangnu are being prepared again. With the rise of feudal consciousness, Meng Jiangnu's reincarnation is really not a strange thing.

Now let us get to know this "Jinan Meng Jiangnu"! Her fiancé, Sun Defu, to whom she "traveled thousands of miles" to join, was forced by the wealthy gentleman Li Baoqing to become a beggar in Jinan. And now the arrogance of wealthy gentlemen and landlords is a common and frequent phenomenon. As a rule, a woman who is praised by reporters in newspapers should be a warrior who bravely fights against wealthy gentlemen, landlords, and the system that produces wealthy gentlemen, but what about our "Jinan Meng Jiangnu"? The reason she became "Jinan Meng Jiangnu" is only because she firmly embraced the determination that a married woman should not eat from two families and went to join her fiancé, Sun Defu, "who was not a free love match but an old-fashioned marriage, so they were still strangers when they met"! If she and Sun Defu really had love and knew each other deeply, her actions would still be a brave warrior who passively refused to cooperate with feudal forces. But even this point is not mentioned!

"Being Laughed at by Feudal Remnants" What Harm! 328

— Qin Yi

After reading Mr. Yu Dafu's "Where Should Chinese Women Run"

Last year's great drought saw the emergence of many women's publications; this year, we can expect favorable weather, and such publications will be like bamboo shoots after a rain. On the first day of the new year, the Women's Ten-Day Profit, which had been suspended for a long time, was revived. The lead article in the content is Yu Dafu's famous article "Where Should Chinese Women Run." Here are a few excerpts:

"Looking at the current situation in China, it seems impossible to completely abandon the family. And women's occupations are not very numerous. Moreover, even male university graduates are sighing about the difficulty of finding employment here, let alone ordinary women."

"My meaning,... may be a bit too old,... unmarried adult women should leave the family; married women should still take care of the family first,... Moreover, China's feudal system has not been completely overthrown: if the housewife of a small family (married women in large families are an exception) runs out regardless of the family, causing the man to suffer the burden of raising children and managing the family, wouldn't she be laughed at by feudal remnants?"

According to Mr. Yu's high opinion, women should generally not run away from the family. After men no longer sigh about "the difficulty of finding employment," there are two types of women who seem to be able to engage in occupations, namely:

(1) Unmarried adult women.

(2) Married women in large families.

And there is one type of woman who he believes should absolutely not engage in occupations, namely:

Housewives of small families.

I want to try to block this high opinion with a mantis arm. Please ask:

(1) In the process of social evolution, should women step into society from the family?

(2) According to the current situation, will there be a day when men's "difficulty in finding employment" is resolved? Can women wait until then to look for occupations!

(3) Large families exist in feudal society. In order for women to have occupations, is it necessary to restore the large family system?

(4) What has become of the people who are afraid of being laughed at by feudal remnants?

(5) Apart from a few people, how many peaceful families are there now that women can be asked to manage?

I dare to answer: for social evolution, women must join society together with men; for women to return to the family is an obstacle to evolution. Chinese society can only have a glimmer of hope if men and women work together to struggle; if feudal poisons are used to confine women, men's "difficulty in finding employment" will probably never be resolved in the current society. As for the large family system, it has become a zombie with the feudal system. If women want to enter that realm, there is no need to talk about occupations. Married women who want to find occupations are mostly those from small families with no relatives to rely on or those with independent personalities. Not letting such people take up occupations is either cutting off their livelihood or destroying their aspirations, which ultimately burdens society.

Moreover, how many peaceful families are there in the current society? Gentlemen just tell women to return to the family, it would be simpler and clearer for beggars to return to the living room. Since the family no longer shelters from wind and sun, and women are not given proper occupations, they can only wander the streets; what is there to talk about regarding morals, order, and safety?

Men always want to maintain their dignity of being served in the family, this is called feudal remnants! Because of these remnants, many women have abandoned their social tasks, and many women have even sadly fallen into the abyss!

Feudal remnants have become something that is not worth mentioning. From the perspective of mutual assistance between men and women, within the possible scope, men in small families should take on some of the work of managing the family. Being laughed at by feudal remnants, may I ask Mr. Yu, who has a reputation, what harm is there?

Talking About Japanese Women's Magazines 329

— Nan Ru

Japan is indeed a country with a relatively high level of culture. Despite the years of economic downturn, various magazines are flourishing like bamboo shoots after a rain. There are also many women's magazines, at least seven or eight times more than in China. "Fujin Koron (Women's Public Opinion)," "Shufu no Tomo (Housewife's Friend)," "Fujinkai (Women's World)," "Fujin no Tomo (Woman's Friend)," "Fujin Gahō (Women's Pictorial)," "Fujin Club (Women's Club)," "Shōjo Club (Girls' Club)" are the most famous monthly magazines, but their content is almost entirely the same: catering to the women of the bourgeoisie. For example, "Shufu no Tomo" and "Fujin Club" are simply the only reading materials for cultivating virtuous mothers and good wives. The text inside is either about how women should obey and be considerate of their husbands, or how to raise children, entertain guests, manage housework, and be a gentle and capable housewife. The majority of readers of these publications are naturally wives, but there are also many unmarried girls who buy them to prepare for being wives. Needless to say, their thinking absolutely advocates men governing the outside and women governing the inside. They see themselves as their husband's wife and their children's mother. Their task is to serve and obey their husband, and bear and raise sons. They don't need other social knowledge, so the content of the publications becomes domestic.

The nature of "Fujin Koron" is somewhat similar to "Chūō Kōron (Central Public Opinion)." Sometimes Yuriko Miyamoto also writes something here, saying a few provocative words in order to awaken a relatively conscious group of women, but the effect is minimal, because the entire publication is based on this doctrine of good wives and wise mothers. Even if you shout until your throat is hoarse, only a few people will hear you.

In a position opposed to the above publications are "Fujin Geijutsu (Women's Literature and Art)," "Josei Bunka (Women's Culture)," and "Kagayaki (Radiance)" published by the Women's Art Society.

These three are all monthly women's cultural magazines. However, "Kagayaki" is very small in size, only half the size of a newspaper, but the text on it is short, concise, and full of social practicality. The editor is Shigure Hasegawa, who is as famous as Kan Kikuchi. Progressive writers such as Yuriko Miyamoto, Ichiko Kamichika, Yasuko Hirabayashi, and Ineko Kubokawa also often contribute articles. This publication was called "Women's Art" three years ago, a thick volume with rich content. I once read three issues. Due to some reason, it has been discontinued for a long time, but according to Hasegawa, it is always possible to resume publication in January or February next year.

"Fujin Geijutsu" is considered the only progressive women's reading material. The editor is Ichiko Kamichika, a famous progressive writer. Since its publication in July last year, it has been published every month in a thick volume without interruption. The content includes literary theory, literary criticism and introduction, creative novels and poems, Q&A, research, etc., focusing on the theory and creation of lower-class women's liberation.

This publication is the only magazine in Japan where progressive female writers can express their opinions, so the content is very rich and the readers are particularly numerous. When it was first published, there were some economic difficulties, but now, because the number of subscribers and buyers is increasing day by day, this problem is no longer a problem. Ichiko Kamichika said: "This publication belongs to Tokyo, to the oppressed women of the world. No matter how bad the environment is, we must continue to struggle. And we hope that international female writers will work with us!"

December 25, 1934, in Tokyo.

For women, can we only be equal to decorations? I ask.

Women's Occupationalists with Double Price 330

— Yi Yi

Selling one's labor to others, and exchanging wages or salaries from others to support oneself, is called an occupation. So, in the current society, engaging in occupational activities, under the condition of being employed, no matter what kind of occupation one is engaged in, one always has to pay a price, which is generally labor.

Selling a portion of labor and obtaining an occupation to make a living is a common phenomenon, but in history, it was very difficult for women to obtain this opportunity. Therefore, in thousands of years of human history, women were raised by men. Although they had labor, there was nowhere to exchange it for an occupation. This is the result of women being oppressed and not getting liberation. In modern times, women can sell their labor and engage in occupations in society. General historians and social problem researchers call this phenomenon one of the facts of women's liberation, which is indeed correct. Because women thereby obtain economic independence and the opportunity to participate in social economic undertakings, changing from people of the family to people of society.

However, modern women occupationalists, especially Chinese women's occupations, although they can gradually engage in occupational activities in society, there are some occupations in which women cannot be like men, only needing to pay the single price of labor to obtain them. They often have to pay a double price than men, that is, in addition to paying labor, they also have to pay a physical appearance price. Therefore, I call this occupation a double-priced occupationalist.

For this type of double-priced occupation, let's temporarily leave aside the female staff in institutions, because although some people say that they are only used as "vases" and rarely pay labor, they are still relatively high-level people, so we are not convenient to say that. There is also another type, which is the female receptionists and singers in various entertainment venues. Although they pay labor under the condition of entertaining guests and singing, they also have to pay a physical appearance price in order to continue in that occupation. However, we will also leave these women aside, because although they are forced to engage in that occupation because of life, the general view of society considers that occupation to be relatively low-class, and it is not good to count it as an example of a proper occupation.

Everyone knows that various companies and stores are magnificent and dignified great business organizations, and are one of the economic lifelines and centers of all cities. The people who serve there, although not very high or very low, can at least be regarded as moderate, proper, and free occupationalists. Therefore, the female staff serving there are called legitimate and justified employees, and no one can say this or that about them. However, in reality, the female shop assistants in these stores are still very pitiful. Obtaining that kind of occupation cannot be the same as men, only paying the price of one kind of labor is enough. They also have to pay a physical appearance price in addition to paying labor, in addition to their main duties of being busy all day, taking goods, writing accounts, and calculating accounts, which is regardless of whether they are willing or not.

When we go to those companies, all the female shop assistants have at least average or above appearance, they all apply powder and rouge, and are deliberately charming. Is it possible that in such a large Shanghai, there are no women with below average appearance? Why are there not a single one in those stores? Is it possible that their income is all very rich? Why can they all dress up like rich wives? It is very obvious that companies and stores originally want to use them as signs. Those who are not young, not beautiful, and not good at dressing up cannot attract employers and do not have the magic of attracting business, so they are naturally in the elimination list. In this way, those women with insufficient appearance, and those who are unwilling to desperately decorate and follow the trend, cannot obtain that kind of occupation. Therefore, not only do those female shop assistants have to treat customers with a humble attitude, but they also welcome all frivolous customers to flock to them, so that the company's business is considerable. This is determined by the improper social psychology of the company, the female shop assistants, and the customers in all aspects, and there is no way to deal with it. However, this psychology and phenomenon fully express the male-centered social thought of treating women as playthings. How can women obtain the same occupation as men? How can they obtain thorough liberation!

A Glimpse of Women's Out-of-School Relief Center 331

— Qian

Out of curiosity and the desire for knowledge, I ran to several women's supplementary schools in a row, but the impression they gave me can be said to be too vague and too clear.

First of all, let's talk about a certain women's supplementary school that has been in Shanghai for two or three years, has a thriving number of students, and recently set up a branch school. On a cloudy and cold day, I walked into the reception room of a certain school's main store. It was a very elegant three-story Western-style building. At the top of the reception room, a large Western piano was squatting majestically. A middle-aged woman in a leather coat was opening the piano with a key. On the right wall of the guest room was a long chair of the kind used in a waiting room, and a young girl was embroidering on the chair; on the left wall were two glass bookcases. In addition to a few dictionaries, "Ciyuan (Etymological Dictionary)," and books such as "Children's World," there were "Liangyou Pictorial," "Times Pictorial," "China Pictorial," and "Movie Pictorial." So many cover beauties filled the bookcase, as if a beauty contest was being held there first.

Because I had to wait for my friend to finish class, I had to stay in the reception room as much as possible, and the playing that hadn't even recognized the staff was drilling into my ears. But during this time, I became familiar with the statistical table on the wall. According to the table, the students' occupations were: merchants accounting for 60%, military and government accounting for 20%, medical and other fields accounting for 15%, and workers accounting for 5%. I thought that it should also be proved here that the above occupation statistics are not the students' own occupations, but 95% are the occupations of their parents or guardians. As for the subjects, there are Chinese, English, arithmetic, embroidery, sewing, music, and bookkeeping. Just as my eyes reached the student's place of origin statistics table, a carriage driver carrying a wool blanket suddenly came in from outside. After a while, a fashionable and wealthy-looking woman walked out from the inside. After she greeted the middle-aged woman playing the piano, the piano-playing woman locked the piano and went to the carriage with her arm in arm. Soon, a bell rang, and my friend also appeared in the guest room, so I went upstairs with her to their dormitory.

The six beds in the dormitory were all arranged in a row against the wall. Not far from the door, there was a long wooden washbasin table, with countless washbasins placed on it. In the center of the room, there were three tables in a row, which were desks for students to study and practice writing. These three desks were ridiculous: one was a small table more than a foot wide and two feet five inches long without drawers. The tabletop was black and white, even uglier than the table in someone's kitchen where the cupboard was placed; the other one was the same size as the first one, but it could be regarded as a small desk in terms of appearance and practice. On this desk, a lady with carefully permed hair was studying hard; as for the third desk, only God knew. A square table with drawers, the style was still the authentic Chinese product from twenty or thirty years ago, the paint was almost completely peeled off, and the color of the exposed wood had turned into a unique brownish-yellow due to years of wiping. These three antiques are where the six resident students in the dormitory prepare their lessons day and night. As for the light above, there was only one dim 25-candlepower electric light.

Speaking of fees, the school's prospectus and my friend's actual situation are as follows: 10 yuan is charged for each subject, and resident students pay an additional 8 yuan per month for accommodation and 8 yuan for meals. In terms of correcting homework, there is a diary every day in Chinese class, but for some reason, the Chinese teacher was replaced three times in less than two months. For those who are just learning to write compositions, the teacher does not revise the sentences for them, but only corrects typos, and some typos are repeatedly allowed to be used by those poor old college students.

Because I was dissatisfied with the first visit, the next day, I set off for another women's supplementary school that had risen suddenly. On this day, I went to class with another girlfriend. Because it was getting late, as soon as my friend walked into the school, she led me to the church upstairs. Along the way, we passed a classroom. The door of the classroom was half open, and I saw two women sitting inside, probably students, and another one pacing on the ground, probably the teacher. They were all wearing silk and fur, like ladies waiting for a wedding feast.

Looking up, I had already arrived at the reception hall downstairs. In the reception hall, which also served as a piano room and reading room, a girl of twenty-seven or eight with a fox stole around her neck was doing the work of just recognizing the staff again. Looking at her anxiousness to speed up and her fingering like playing the organ, I really wanted to persuade her to abandon that kind of decoration and learn some other useful knowledge, oh! Unfortunately, I don't know her!

Here, because another group of people have classes here at night, the books and newspapers on display are very progressive. Just as I was engrossed in reading an article, a female clerk walked out of the office. She stared at me up and down for several minutes before turning around and returning to the office. So, like looking in a mirror, I hurriedly took my eyes back and looked at myself. I thought I was dressed very neatly, but at this time, under the polishing of other mountains, I realized that I looked like an ugly duckling. Not only was a coat old, but the material and style were too outdated. A pair of broken leather shoes was simply like a tattered shoe. On the way home, I thought of those poor women who had dropped out of school who didn't even have old coats and broken leather shoes to wear. Learn.

Autobiography of a "Social Person" 332

— Hua

Two weeks of private tutoring life

Several encounters of looking for a job

Recognition of a real "social person"

How I transformed into a social person, after gathering all kinds of oppression from social customs, parental surveillance, and the imprisonment of husbands and children, and how I fought to complete it, that's all in the past.

The most interesting thing was in the summer of 1930, when the wave of unemployment swept me from Anhui to Shanghai. At that time, I was really ridiculously poor. I was eating by boarding with friends, and I found a place to live near my friends. The four walls were all concrete, because it was not a garret, but a bathroom without a bathtub. A canvas bed and three boxes were arranged in a bright and compact way, but unfortunately, there were no tables and chairs, which aroused the suspicion of the second landlord, who often sent me out with probing eyes and welcomed me back with careless eyes.

I read the self-introduction column of Shen Bao with the greatest attention every day, but after two weeks, I still couldn't find a job suitable for me. Sometimes, I would sit at the home of my father's friend. The gorgeous sofa and hypocritical hospitality made me feel very strange. When I saw those poor insects waiting for jobs behind the hall, a kind of embarrassing and helpless expression made my heart clench. I returned with my disappointed heart, wandering the streets again.

The heat gradually subsided, and cicadas chirped on the treetops. One afternoon, this friend of my father came to me. He said:

"Go and teach the three children of Military Commander ×. Although the salary is only 60 yuan, you only teach history, geography, and arithmetic for three hours a day. Chinese and English are taught by male teachers. However, Military Commander × wants the female teacher to be able to live in his house, so that she can take care of the children at any time. - I think, there is nothing you can't do, right?"

Of course, I had to agree. Military Commander × was also a friend of my father.

The life of this family was very extravagant and dissolute. The old man was a retired military commander, lying in bed smoking opium every day; the housework was managed by his wife; there were two or three young concubines to relieve boredom; there were slaves at home, and cars with bodyguards when going out. They had plenty of foreign money, and anything he wanted could be satisfied.

But for me, this was simply a living hell. Although teaching only took three hours, the spoiled children were so incompetent; and outside of class, I had to chat with the wife and play cards with the concubines, endlessly consuming my time, often until the late and tired night; I couldn't read a book at all, or do anything of my own.

I really hated myself: "Is my entire time only worth 60 yuan? "Playing with things loses one's ambition." Why did I bother to leave home? Go away, this is definitely not the place for me to solve the problem of eating!"

So, after only two weeks, I couldn't stay any longer, and I resolutely walked out of this deep den of sin.

Returning to the real garret, I regained my true form and lived very soberly again. One day, I found an advertisement in the newspaper for a music company to recruit staff. The qualifications for the staff were to have basic knowledge of music theory and to have taught music before. I thought I was very confident in this; I immediately wrote a letter of application, even though the salary was only 30 yuan.

A reply came three days later. Following this reply, I walked into a large ballroom, where thirty or forty young women, dressed in gorgeous clothes, were sitting. I looked intently and saw that there was only one, just one, as honest as we were, matching our coarse cloth clothes; I took a deep breath: "What are we here to do? Will she and I have hope?"

The exam was very simple: a young man with very shiny hair and a powdered face sat by the organ, playing harmonies, and asked about the organization of the sound by name. I paid attention to hearing each person's answer. Everyone had mistakes, but the degree of mistakes was different; but to my surprise, that honest fellow didn't make any mistakes at all.

Walking out, my heart was very relaxed, and I felt very sure that since they were recruiting six people, she and I would definitely be secure. However, a week passed, two weeks, three weeks passed, and forever, I never received a reply from that music company again.

At the same time, I was preparing to apply for a silk weaving factory. This disappointment and injustice were forgotten in my rush to run around with my 20 yuan deposit.

Thanks to the mutual care and support of friends, I actually took the 20 yuan and mixed into another group of starving people.

We were called one by one in front of the gentleman and the foreman, and their eyes shone straight at the body of each person being called, from head to toe, and then carefully examined their hands.

"You've read books, right?..." they asked me, and seemed to be discussing with each other.

"Unreliable, troublemaker!..." another pot-bellied man with fierce eyes said.

Like this, I was waved out the door.

I thought: "The company thinks I'm not pretty; but here they think my hands are a little delicate, "unreliable, troublemaker"; - in the current society, what is the meaning of women's existence!"

Now, although I am economically independent, sex and occupation are absolutely free, and I am personally a liberated social person; but eating is for living, and living is not for eating. As a social person, how can I live my social life without being satisfied with personal liberation and losing the social meaning of my life - this is the content of my real life.

Society is not a women's society. For a social woman, slandering women with the "old morality" that binds women has almost become a universal phenomenon. For me, this is discarded beside me like a pile of garbage; it seems that these obvious things have not fooled me. The most terrible thing is the new deception of new-style life; warmth and tranquility make women unconsciously lose the courage to face the hardships of reality; and in the praise of "great lovers," how many women sacrifice themselves; and how many women are tossed about in the famine of occupations, ignoring their surroundings, not recognizing the structure of the real society, so that they deviate from the development of themselves and society and become prisoners of occupation - I, of course, am no exception. After entering society, these traps are laid out on my future. They look like a lush green grassland, but as long as you hesitate, you will fall into an invisible trap; climbing out of one trap after another constantly requires your own struggle and your own fight.

In this stage of life, the old society scolds me as a traitor, and friends in the new society (?) regard me as a fickle and unreliable woman; in all the eyes cast on me, I can feel a kind of mocking and insulting spark. I always believe that the greatness of survivors is great social undertakings. Only in this kind of undertaking can there be one's own existence, and can the brilliance of the relationship between people be discovered. At that time - I thank these evaluations and attacks that promote me to use careful attention to understand and analyze myself and society; the truth rescued me: "Oppressed women, must recognize the direction to go from the essence of social phenomena, and the causal laws of social phenomena, recognize the truth to liberate our entire self! Fight ruthlessly against all new and old bad environments!"

This inner cleansing was indeed a big change for me. The unprincipled disputes growing in my heart, the atmosphere of depression and misery in life, I have converted to this understanding of truth and have obtained clear liberation; I, with a truly individual, conscious life, now and in the future, provide a bright illumination to guide me; a flower of unwavering joy is always blooming in my heart.

On the other hand, unemployment and hunger still follow me like a shadow, which is precisely a huge persecution suffered by general social women! Occupations are so difficult to obtain, and occupational wages are particularly lower than those of men; especially, women's occupations - such as clerks, shop assistants, etc. - are decorated with a sexual insulting nature, which is so infuriating!

However, this is not a matter of emotional indignation. Precisely because women now are still rarely people of society; they are slaves of the family, of husbands or lovers, of children, of private property and occupation; therefore, women who step into society suffer all kinds of persecution and abuse. For our own sake, for the future of our women, we must break through these barriers! Socially meaningful, human labor, resistance, fighting, until we stand in society like men. - In this way, women create their own, the real meaning of social people!
